The Fifth Ward Cracks Down on a Drug Organization 158

A woman named Xu Liu, hid twelve ounces of morphine on her person last Friday while traveling in the Public Concession. She was discovered by investigators and taken to the police station. She confessed that the drugs were purchased from the home of Yongren Xu Shilong at No. 3, Jiwufang, Ximen Road, French Concession. Thereupon, the Public Concession Police notified the French Concession Police, and detective Lu Zhulin, deputy detective Wang Rusong, Zhang Daorong, and Bao Tang Liu Jinrong of the Second Investigation Group rushed to search the premises. The old Xu Shilong had already fled upon hearing the news. Only Xu's younger brother, Xu Wenxing, the clerk Xu Weicheng, and buyers Wang Fuming, Wang Wenkui, Ding Liangcheng, Zhang Yichun, Zhang Weixin, Qiu Wenbiao, Jiang Shanqi, Wang Yousan, Zhang Fanggui, and eleven others were arrested. Five small packages of heroin, five empty tin boxes for packing morphine, coffee essence, white glue powder, one thousand yuan in silver dollars, three account books, a tin of red pill biscuits, three pill-making boards, and raw materials for red pills were seized. They were all taken back to the police station for detention. Yesterday, they were sent to the First Criminal Court of the Second Special District Court, where they were interrogated by Judge Xiong Huiping. The police lawyer Yao Zhaodi stated that the police had not yet completed the investigation of the case and that the principal offender was at large. He requested a postponement to arrest the principal offender and clarify the facts before requesting a hearing. He also presented the evidence to the court. The detective reported on the arrest of the defendants and the search process. The court verified the report and briefly interrogated the defendants before ordering a postponement for further investigation. The defendants were returned to the police station for detention.

Sentenced to Two Months Imprisonment 159

Zhang Genshou, an apprentice from Suzhou at Yifaxiang Water Shop, opposite the Shiliupu Tram Station in the French Concession, 18 years old this year, previously teased and sucked the semen of Huang Hengtai, a 15-year-old apprentice from Ningbo, more than ten times, causing his glans to swell and making it difficult for him to walk. Assassination Case

Accomplice Jiang Yinlong's Appeal Rejected 160

Previously, Lü Cai, a native of Ninghai, Zhejiang, who was involved in the underworld in Deshanli, French Avenue, was killed because his wife was taken by his apprentice Wang Damao. Later, Lü also took Gu Qiaozi, the lover of another apprentice, Hou Chunrong. As a result, Lü was lured by Wang and Hou to Kangti Road, French Concession, where he was hacked to death with knives and axes, suffering twenty-three axe wounds and eight knife wounds all over his body. The murderers fled the scene. Later, the police transported the body to the coroner's office. After the court verified the body and determined that there were no relatives, it was handled by the charity hall. Subsequently, the deceased's father, Lü Arong, found out and reported it to the police, who arrested Jiang Yinlong (21 years old, a razor shop assistant from Zhenglai Xing, Mofang Street, Suzhou), an accomplice in the case, and sent him to the Second Special District Court. After investigation, Jiang was sentenced to twelve years in prison for joint murder. Jiang was dissatisfied with the original judgment and filed an appeal with the Third Branch of the Jiangsu Higher Court. The court, headed by Presiding Judge Zhou, with Judges Guo and Fan and Prosecutor Zhang, held a collegial panel for the trial and declared the debate closed. The judgment was announced yesterday morning: the appellant's appeal was rejected. After the judgment, the appellant was returned to the detention center to await execution after the third-instance appeal period.

The Entire Station Building Has Been Completed 161

The Ministry of Railways Will Send Personnel to Inspect and Accept It in Two Days

The Transportation Department Plans to Move in on the First of Next Month

After the January 28th Incident, the Shanghai North Station was nine-tenths destroyed. After the war subsided, the two railway bureaus slightly opened a portion of the original site and repaired it to provide a place for passengers to rest. As for the entire North Station, it has been rebuilt for more than two months and was completely completed yesterday. The Ministry of Railways plans to send personnel to accept it in two days. The Transportation Department of the Railway Bureau will also move in to work on the first of next month. The entire building is magnificent. Although it only has two floors, it is tall and majestic, and the atmosphere is grand. This type of three-dimensional architecture is not common in China. The details are recorded as follows:

Completely Completed 162

The Shanghai North Station was built by the Zhongnan Construction Company. From the start of construction to the present, it will take three months, with a total cost of tens of thousands of yuan. The internal layout is slightly different from the old station. The entire building is three-dimensional, and the exterior is made of large red concrete blocks. The entrance faces west, with the four large black characters "Shanghai North Station". The interior was completed earlier, but the electrical and water lines were only installed yesterday. The appearance is completely new compared to before, and it is no longer a scene of broken walls.

Sending Personnel for Inspection and Acceptance 163

After the completion of the project, the two railway bureaus sent personnel to inspect it and found it satisfactory. It was decided to submit a request to the Ministry of Railways on the 31st of this month (the day after tomorrow) to send personnel for inspection and acceptance. The Transportation Department of the two railway bureaus was originally located at the North Station. After the station was destroyed, a temporary and simple site was built near the Boundary Road Station for office work. With the completion of the new site, it will be moved back on the first of next month.

Page 14

Forced Membership in Trade Associations

Should Request Administrative Agencies to Execute 164

Trade Associations Write to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce Yesterday

The Shanghai Municipal Trade Associations previously drafted measures for compulsory membership of fellow traders, which were submitted to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce for instructions. They have been submitted to the Executive Yuan for referral to the Legislative Yuan for attention during the revision of laws and regulations. However, it was heard yesterday that the Intestine Industry, Sino-Foreign General Merchandise Industry, Cosmetics Industry, and other trade associations believe that Article 7 of the Law on Trade Associations of Industry and Commerce has been revised last year, and fellow traders "shall" join the association. The wording is affirmative, and the procedure for the case has reached the stage where administrative agencies should execute it, without the need to refer it to the Legislative Yuan. Therefore, they jointly sent a letter to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, the original text of which is as follows: "To the esteemed Chamber, regarding the case, it was found on October 15, 1932, that your esteemed Chamber received a letter from the Social Affairs Bureau, No. 4640, which stated that the Municipal Government's order No. 2890 stated that the Executive Yuan's order No. 3893 stated that the National Government's order No. Lu Zi 238 stated that the Law on Trade Associations of Industry and Commerce had been formulated and promulgated, and that Article 7 of the law had been revised and should be implemented. In addition to separate orders, the revised article is hereby copied for your information and to instruct your subordinates to take note. This order includes the revised Article 7 of the Law on Trade Associations of Industry and Commerce: 'Companies and firms in the same industry shall be members of the trade association and send representatives to attend meetings, except for those who have been expelled.' It is believed that the law is the binding rule of the state, and once it is formulated, promulgated, and implemented, the administrative agencies bear the responsibility of execution, without waiting for any request. Otherwise, how can the effectiveness of the law be generated? If the law is not enforced, it will not only become a mere formality but also lose the authority of the administration. Article 7 of the Law on Trade Associations of Industry and Commerce has been revised from 'may' to 'shall,' and the wording is affirmative. Fellow traders shall join the association. In other words, administrative agencies have the power to compel fellow traders who do not join the association to join. If they are still not bound by the law, wouldn't it make the law-abiding fellow traders feel that their rights and obligations are unequal, and both the spirit of the law and the authority of the administration would be lost? Previously, various trade associations jointly drafted a proposal to urge fellow traders

to join the association, 'Because the people have an obligation to abide by national laws and regulations, the competent authorities should announce it, limit the time for joining the association, and, if they do not comply after the deadline, they will be prosecuted for resisting the national administrative power and forced to join the association.' The foolish opinions of our associations are deemed appropriate. Later, on June 26 of this year, the Ministry of Industry and Commerce issued a letter No. Shang Zi 18496, stating that it had been noted that the matters mentioned have been submitted to the Executive Yuan by the Ministry in a separate case for referral to the Legislative Yuan for attention when revising the regulations, hoping to obtain appropriate relief measures. This order and other reasons were received. After reading it, we were shocked. It was found that Article 7 of the Law on Trade Associations of Industry and Commerce has been revised by the Legislative Yuan, and the National Government's order No. Lu Zi 238 has ordered its implementation, and the case files are available for reference. The process of referring this case to the Legislative Yuan is puzzling. It is feared that the Ministry of Industry and Commerce is negligent in examining the procedures of this case, or some people say that supplementary regulations should be included in the implementation rules of the Trade Association Law in order to make Article 7 of the Trade Association Law effective. However, it is not known that the effectiveness of joining the association depends entirely on the provisions of Article 7 of the Trade Association Law, as proven by those who have already joined the association, and it has nothing to do with the implementation rules. Otherwise, all the fellow traders who have joined the association can make excuses that there are no supplementary provisions in the implementation rules and withdraw from the association. Moreover, the implementation rules are only a supporting law to the Trade Association Law. A review of the regulations revised and promulgated by the Ministry on July 25, 1930,

mainly regulates the organization of the association, the dispatch of members, and the subordination of government offices. At that time, the matter was just being initiated, or there were matters not specified in detail in the Association Law, so it was necessary to have these implementation rules as supplements. Now, the revised wording of Article 9 is clear, so what is the need for supplements? Or some people say that the word "shall" in Article 7 should be revised to "must" in order to solve the problem. This is an overcorrection and ignores the purpose of legislation and usage. It is important to know that the presence of the word "shall" in the law is already effective. What is the use of repeated applications with different words but the same meaning, which only reveals the pedantry of their documentary knowledge? Once a law is promulgated and implemented, it has binding effect. If fellow traders are still allowed not to join the association, those who have already joined will inevitably withdraw, and there will never be any hope for a healthy association. The so-called construction undertaking will become a mere illusion, and even the association will be disintegrated, and the foundation of the chamber of commerce will be shaken. This is not just a problem for the Shanghai area but will affect the whole country. Looking ahead, we are extremely worried. It is hoped that your esteemed Chamber, with its usual

wisdom, will see this early on. May we rely on your great power to dispatch representatives to petition the Executive Yuan and order the Shanghai Municipal Government to enforce it according to the previously drafted measures in order to maintain the effectiveness of the law and demonstrate the authority of the administration."

Old Deeds in the Central District

The Land Bureau Urges Payment for Land Redemption 167

According to the Guo Wen News Agency, the new Shanghai Municipal Government building will be inaugurated on October 10th, and the office will be moved in on New Year's Day of the 23rd year. However, private construction is crucial to the prosperity of the central district, but construction is still not common. According to the Shanghai Central District Landowners Association, the land ownership certificates from the Land Bureau have not yet been fully issued. Land disputes have not been resolved, so construction is out of the question. Yesterday, reporters specifically inquired about the truth from the Land Bureau. According to staff at the Land Bureau, the Land Bureau is redeeming the old deeds held by old landowners, but many have left Shanghai or are waiting to see what happens and have not yet submitted their deeds. As a result, land ownership certificates cannot be issued rashly, to avoid disputes with two landowners for the same plot of land. However, in this situation, old landowners cannot privately transfer the land, so even if they delay in an attempt to avoid this, it is futile.

The Bureau has already drafted a method and submitted it to the municipal government, stating that in addition to submitting the old deeds for the expropriated land for redemption, all matters related to the ownership of the land should be handled by the Ministry of Interior. The Ministry of Interior then submitted a request to the Executive Yuan for instructions, which has been delayed and has not yet been approved. However, recently, several people have come to the Bureau every day to submit their deeds for inspection. Once the Bureau verifies that they are correct, it will immediately issue a certificate for claiming payment, directing them to the Finance Bureau to collect the land price.

Regulations of the Ministry of Railways

Measures for Employee, Chief, and Police Uniforms 169

Effective from September 1st

Instructions to the Two-Way Railway Bureau to Comply With

The Ministry of Railways instructed the Two-Way Railway Bureau, stating that the various uniforms issued to employees, chiefs, and police officers of each route often lack a fixed schedule, leading to requests being submitted at the last minute or rushed purchases due to time constraints. Furthermore, each route bids for various materials, and requests the Ministry to send personnel to supervise the bidding. Sometimes, due to time constraints, the Ministry is unable to send personnel, and each route conducts its own bidding. All these situations have many drawbacks. In order to rectify this, except for various projects and materials used for driving that need to be purchased temporarily or urgently,

The uniforms that should be issued to employees in the vehicle and machinery departments, as well as various materials for daily use that can be purchased and manufactured on time, now have a fixed schedule and methods, which are listed separately as follows:

Employee Uniforms 170

Previously, it was stipulated that the period for manufacturing and issuing summer uniforms for railway police uniforms was from March to April each year, and the period for manufacturing and issuing winter uniforms was from September to October. The situation for other employees who were issued winter and summer uniforms was the same as that of the railway police. In the future, each route should manufacture and issue various employee uniforms according to the above-mentioned schedule, and submit a request for purchase in accordance with the regulations. For employee teams and police officers who are issued uniforms for both spring and autumn seasons, it is also stipulated that the period for manufacturing and issuing spring uniforms is from January to February each year, and the period for manufacturing and issuing autumn uniforms is from July to August each year. However, requests must be submitted to the Ministry for approval one month in advance.

Various Materials 171

Each route should order all materials, except in special circumstances or due to limited financial resources, that cannot be purchased and used on schedule. For those that are regularly ordered for daily use in the industrial and mechanical departments for road maintenance, each year should be divided into four periods, with three months per period, and requests should be submitted for purchase on schedule. The materials department of each route should first notify the purchasing agency of the quantity of materials needed every three months, and then the purchasing agency should submit a request for purchase in accordance with the regulations during the stipulated period. However, the deadline for submitting requests should be two months before each period. If it is necessary to order from overseas, the request should be submitted to the Ministry at least six months before each period.

Supervise Bidding 172

The materials purchased by each route on its own that require the Ministry

to send personnel to supervise the bidding must be submitted to the Ministry for approval two weeks before the bidding. For items that have been specifically approved by the Ministry to be tendered by the route itself, the members of the bidding supervision committee should be designated in advance when the route is notified, to avoid being rushed. All the above-mentioned regulations should be implemented separately from September 3rd of this year, and the implementation situation should be reported in advance. In addition to separate orders, it is hoped that they will be strictly followed. This order.

Methods for Existing Companies to Submit Supplementary Registration

The Ministry of Industry and Commerce Orders the Commercial Federation to Notify 173

The Ministry of Industry and Commerce issued an order to the National Federation of Chambers of Commerce yesterday, stating that existing companies that have not registered must apply for registration in accordance with the law before September 30th of this year. The Ministry of Industry and Commerce stated: "It has already been notified that existing companies that have not registered must apply for registration in accordance with the law before September 30th of this year. Now, according to the report from the Beijing Municipal Social Affairs Bureau, the Beijing Municipal Factory Federation has reported that it is requesting a special method for supplementing the required documents for the registration of existing companies, such as the inspection certificate from the competent official, the investigation report from the directors and supervisors, and the resolution of the founding meeting. After investigation, it has been determined that existing companies have generally been established for many years, and they did not apply for management in accordance with the company law when they were originally established. Therefore, the registration documents currently prepared cannot be consistent with the original ones. In order to comply with the facts and the law, a special method of submitting supplementary registration documents for existing companies is hereby formulated in four articles. A copy of the method is enclosed, and the association is notified to forward it. This is hereby notified. A copy of the method is attached." Method for Existing Companies to Submit Supplementary Registration Documents: ⑴ If the shares of an existing company are fully subscribed by the promoters, the competent authority should be requested to inspect them in accordance with the law and issue an inspection certificate; ⑵ If the shares of an existing company are not fully subscribed by the promoters, the current directors and supervisors should reinvestigate and issue a report, and request the shareholders' meeting to approve it; ⑶ The resolution of the founding meeting may be replaced by the resolution of the shareholders' meeting of the most recent revised articles of association, the resolution of the shareholders' meeting to elect the current board of directors and supervisors, and the resolution of the shareholders' meeting to approve the investigation report of the directors and supervisors prior to that; ⑷ For the procedures in the first and second articles, if an existing company cannot apply for registration within the time limit, it may state the reasons within the time limit and formally apply for registration after the time limit. However, the time must be stated in advance and approved by the Ministry of Industry and Commerce.

Robbery at Hu's House in Wusong 174

Police and Local Defense Corps Respond to the Alarm and Pursue

Robbers Open Fire and Resist Arrest

At about 0:30 AM yesterday, eight robbers suddenly came to the residence of Zhang Baogen and Zhang Wenlai at No. 10, Hujia Port, Wusong, each armed with pistols and wooden sticks, their faces painted with makeup. They broke into the house, immediately tied up the victims, and broke the arm of the old woman Zhang Yang and injured the head of the relative Yang Huilai, forcing them to reveal the location of the silver dollars. As a result, property worth about 400 or 500 yuan was robbed. After the incident, the victims beat gongs to report to the police. Yang Wenbin, the platoon leader of the 3rd platoon of the local defense corps in the nearby 7th Public Security District, and others, dispatched police and local defense corps members to pursue the robbers in all directions. They were chased near the west of Hujia Port by the local defense corps. The robbers opened fire to resist arrest. Corps member Yang Caixian drew his gun and returned fire, but it was dark and the robbers escaped to the west. At 8:00 AM yesterday, the incident was reported to Gong Erkui, the district chief of the 7th Public Security District, who ordered his subordinates to search for the robbers.

Two Fires 175

At about 8:50 PM last night, a fire broke out at the residence of No. 9, Xie Xing Li, Gonghe Road, Zhabei, due to carelessness. Thick smoke filled the air and flames soared, spreading to the two neighboring households, Nos. 10 and 11. Firefighters arrived and extinguished the fire at 10:30 PM. Three rooms were destroyed. The person responsible for the fire has been detained by the patrol police and handed over to the 4th Public Security Bureau for investigation.

At 12:15 AM the night before last night, a sudden fire broke out at the Hua Cheng Knitting Factory, No. 2, Tongle Li, West Meixie Road, in front of the Nanshi Local Court, and quickly spread. Due to the heavy rain, there was a lack of rescuers and the fire was fierce, spreading to No. 1 and the back of the Xiangxing Pawnshop along the road. Firefighters arrived and put out the fire in time, preventing it from spreading. However, houses No. 1 and 2 were completely destroyed, and the back of Xiangxing Pawnshop was burned. The fire chief was summoned by the 2nd Police Station yesterday for investigation.

Famous Doctor Huang Yunzhong Arrives in Shanghai from Beijing 176

The Central National Medical Museum has been researching various scientific principles in recent years with great success. Yesterday, Zhang Yunzhong, the director of the Beijing Ophthalmology Hospital, arrived in Beijing, carrying his writings over the years and more than 100 newly invented anatomical diagrams, and handed them over to the National Medical Museum for research. Jiao Yitang, the director of the museum, believed that Mr. Zhang was a well-known Western doctor who could deeply study the theories of divergence and use scientific methods to create diagrams to prove the theories of meridians and collaterals, the five elements, and the Qi transformation in ancient Chinese medicine. It was truly an unprecedented invention. On August 20, a special research meeting was held at the National Medical Museum. Those present included Chen Lifu, Ye Guren, Zhang Yunzhong, and Ms. Lun Lingfei. All agreed that the theories of Chinese medicine had been scientifically proven, which was of great significance to the future of Chinese medicine. It is heard that Mr. Zhang has returned to Guangdong to visit his relatives and has now arrived in Shanghai from Beijing. According to Mr. Zhang, countries around the world have been actively researching Chinese medicine recently, and the League of Nations Conference has also had a proposal to study ancient Chinese medicine, which shows that Chinese medicine has an international trend. We can take this opportunity to vigorously clarify the scientific principles of Chinese medicine and win honor for our national academic community in the world. Ms. Lun is the wife of Du Lüsheng, a female disciple of the poet Kuang Feng, who is good at lyrics and painting. She has a deep understanding of Chinese medicine and has been studying Western medicine methods with Dr. Zhang Yunzhong in Beijing for the past few years. She has drawn more than 100 anatomical diagrams based on the principles clarified by Zhang, and has submitted them to the Central National Medical Museum. The director of the museum, Jiao Yitang, and others respect her talent, so they invited Ms. Lun to attend the research conference.

Sometimes, when foreign goods have not arrived and China urgently needs makeup, it is really impossible to buy them with money. Although it is not perfect, he continues to work hard and strive for excellence, hoping to achieve at least the same results as imported products. Now he has sent many samples to Lianhua, Tianyi, Yueming, Yihua, and other film companies for trial use. Publishing Industry 179

Publication of Supplement to Interpretation of Laws: The "Compilation of Unified Interpretations of the National Government" compiled by Yu Zhongluo, former Standing Committee Member of the Shanghai Lawyers Association, Wu Xuepeng, Secretary, etc., has now completed the supplement. It includes all the interpretation documents promulgated from Yuanzi No. 648 to No. 838 (21st year). It is a thick volume of sixteen-size newspaper, which is bound and classified according to current laws and regulations, and is arranged in the order of chapters, sections, and articles for easy inspection. For each category, the publication, implementation, or invalidation date of the law is noted in detail to clarify the evolution. The original text includes the letters and telegrams interpreting the law and the original documents requesting interpretation, numbered sequentially, and complete from beginning to end. The index is listed according to the interpretation number, with a summary of the main points and the relevant legal provisions and original page numbers attached. Those who know the interpretation number but do not know the content can easily find it. This book is now published and sold at the Shanghai Lawyers Association. The cost of the supplement is one yuan. If you want to buy it together with the previous compilation (three volumes), the original price of four yuan will still be charged. If you buy the two compilations together, you will receive a 20% discount. In addition, postage will be charged.

Spring and Autumn

The Year's Various Things 188

— Nineteen

This year is a "National Products Year," which has been generally recognized. However, observing from various aspects, it seems that this year is not just a "National Products Year," because, examining the domestic situation, there are really too many events. For example, with the Tanggu Truce, the national crisis can be temporarily declared over; therefore, this year can be called "Truce Year," or "End of National Crisis Year." Now that the national crisis has ended, there is no need to "repel" externally, but it is greatly possible to "settle" internally! Therefore, this year can also be called "Internal Pacification Year." The government will seek unification through construction, and it cannot but borrow talents from other countries; thus, technical personnel from the League of Nations are about to come to China to cooperate with our country, opening a new record in our country's history. This year can also be called "League of Nations Cooperation Year." Since the opening of the aviation donation, the common people have been able to deeply understand the greater good and reluctantly loosen their purse strings. This is also a matter worthy of commemoration. If we say that this year is "Aviation Year," who would say it is inappropriate? Furthermore, our country's finances have reached the extreme of difficulty. Since the source cannot be increased, the outflow cannot but be reduced. Therefore, the expenses of various agencies are all reduced and issued; and the salaries of service personnel are discounted by 20% or 30%. Therefore, this year can also be called "Austerity Year."

The price cut is incredibly cheap, but American wheat has been ordered and is about to be imported; therefore, calling this year "Year of Cheap Grain" is also acceptable; calling it "Year of American Wheat Imports" is also not impossible. Advertisements for greatly reduced-price cloth attract people in the cities. It is said that Indian silk, as thin as paper, is only worth two or three jiao per foot. Other silk fabrics and daily necessities are also unusually cheap. Therefore, this year can also be called "Year of Cheap Prices" or "Year of Bargains."

If we say that this year is "Year of Examinations," I think a generation of future masters will nod in agreement. From graduation to further education, statistically, they have to go through three types of examinations at school: the final examination, the entrance examination, and the entrance examination for further education 丨 The various tests before graduation are not included. In addition, the higher and ordinary qualification examinations held by various provinces to seek talents for the country have already been held, and some are about to be held. Since there are so many examinations, this year can also be called "Year of Examinations."

There is also a "Year of Bonuses," which Rongyu Jun has already described in detail, see the ninth issue of this publication, so I will not waste any more words.

The Mystery of Shanghai 189

— Xianxian

There are many people who oppose the golden rule that Shanghai is full of gold, but there are still many people who believe that Shanghai is full of gold is an indelible saying. In Shanghai, just posting a recruitment advertisement with a brief description of the duties and a monthly allowance of ten yuan, in less than half a day, there will be bundles of application letters coming to apply. If you post an advertisement seeking a job, except for women, waiting for a year and a half, most likely no one will ask. If you take a stroll on the street, you will see countless beggars teetering on the brink of starvation, putting on a dignified appearance that is both like crying and like laughing, reaching out to people to beg for a penny's worth of alms. From the magnificent grand hotels in the evening to the entrances of small alleys without even gas lamps, they are crowded with sellers of flesh. They cannot find bread and have to trade the flesh passed down from their parents. These, though just a few examples, have everywhere exposed the poverty of Shanghai. In Shanghai, not only can you not pick up gold, but you are also in danger of being swallowed by Shanghai.

However, looking at the same problem from another side of society, there are different opinions. The unemployed read the advertisements, and if they can run faster than others, they can get a position with a monthly salary of ten yuan. Posting a job-seeking advertisement, if the opportunity is good, can also solve the unemployment problem, especially women's job-seeking advertisements, which are even more effective. Begging does not require capital, knowledge, or labor; as long as you can put on a face that is both like crying and like laughing, you can maintain life. These few examples have everywhere demonstrated that Shanghai is not poor and that Shanghai is full of gold. Every day, countless people who pick up gold come to Shanghai. Every day, countless people leave Shanghai with their pockets full or without picking up a single big one. Many people are loudly shouting about economic oppression and unemployment panic, but Shanghai's population is increasing year by year, and it is not often heard that people starve to death.

Is Shanghai really full of gold? This is truly an age-old mystery.

Psychological Testing of Women 190

— A-jie

Psychologists only know "Child Psychology," "Criminal Psychology," and "Abnormal Psychology," as well as "Personality Type," "Subconsciousness," "Hallucination," "Illusion," "Emotion," "Concept," and so on. The psychology of women has not been thoroughly studied. Although the Chinese philosopher Li Shicen and the Russian Rasputin have deeply researched women's psychology, it is difficult to say that they have truly mastered it. Therefore, Confucius said: "Women and petty people are difficult to deal with!" Poets say: "A thousand pieces of gold cannot buy a beauty's heart." This is the reason.

After all, Germans have high academic knowledge. According to a Berlin telegram: "The German government has recently established a 'Women's Fashion Bureau,' which is headed by the wife of the current Minister of Propaganda and Culture, Goebbels. The bureau will hold a clothing material exhibition in mid-August, and is currently actively preparing for it. It is said that this attempt is actually to reform the psychology of modern women, arouse the characteristics of the German nation, and advance in parallel with the new German trend." From this news, isn't it possible to test women's psychology through clothing? To change women's psychology, one should start by reforming women's clothing.

Length can be measured; weight can be weighed; quantity can be counted; only "beauty" and "ugliness" have no standard instrument to test. Therefore, women in India and Africa also have beauties that can topple cities and countries. Male dogs look at female dogs, and roosters look at hens, and they all seem beautiful. Thirty or forty years ago, Suzhou head, Yangzhou feet, wide borders, false tails, wasn't that the standard for beautiful women's attire? Now, from short clothes and narrow sleeves, it has slowly changed to bare feet and exposed bodies. Perhaps in the near future, "nudity" will be practiced, returning to the era of the original human. What is the psychology of women? I am not a psychology expert, so I cannot answer.

Perhaps it is said that this is because people's hearts are changing from "pure and honest" to "shallow and frivolous," and women's virtues are changing from "chaste and virtuous" to "licentious and dissolute." I don't think so. This phenomenon is indeed a sign of civilized progress and a precursor to universal harmony. Why? For example, now foreigners can use cellulose from the plant kingdom to manufacture viscose and cellulose acetate, drawing it into extremely thin strands, which is called "rayon." Women make clothes with it, and how beautiful and lovely they are. Domestic silk fabrics have naturally become old grannies with wrinkled skin and white hair, and they are about to fall behind. If someone invents "glass silk" and studies and applies salts such as silicic acid, phosphoric acid, boric acid, and tungstic acid, then its convenience will be even greater than "rayon." 1. There is no need to wash it; just burn it once with fire, and it will be like new, which is extremely suitable for the current lazy women's psychology, right? 2. Rich in carnal feeling: wearing clothes made of "glass" naturally has a rich carnal feeling, no less than the beauty of curves. Even if the authorities want to ban "nude sports," "glass clothes" can also cope with it. Isn't it extremely suitable for the current carnal women's psychology? These are all good signs of civilized progress. It is truly unjust to add the crimes of "shallow" and "licentious" to the heads of modern women!

Illness 191

— Ye Gu

At a friend's house, there is a female servant employed; now this female servant is sick; suffering from a very serious illness. Yellow face, listless spirit, everywhere shows that she has no strength; no strength to do the work. Logically, even if she cannot stay in the hospital for treatment, she should go back to her hometown to rest; but in fact, she has no money to recuperate, and because there is a lazy husband who smokes opium in her distant home, she has to endure the entanglement of the disease and work hard for a living!

Every day, early in the morning, when people are in good dreams, she gets up early, empties chamber pots, cooks breakfast, wipes tables, and sweeps the floor, non-stop. Then she buys groceries, cooks lunch, washes clothes, and cooks dinner. When the masters play mahjong, she serves them during the day, and she also serves them late at night, until the masters go to sleep, and then she goes to sleep! The next day, it's like this again, doing heavy work like cattle and horses!

Oh! Although she is sick now, so sick that she has no strength at all; but for her own life and the life of her husband, she has to endure the sick body and work! If she doesn't work, there is no food to eat; and who will do the work for the masters? If she hires a substitute, the wages belong to someone else; then what about herself?

Oh! I really don't know how many poor people there are in the world! Poor people! For every day's life, if they don't work and don't labor, there is no food to eat; therefore, every day, they have to sell their strength, their body! To do heavy work like cattle and horses!

Oh! Poor people, laborers who sell their physical strength, should not be able to get sick; if they get sick, they cannot work; for a living, even if they are sick, they have to work; then, in the end, it is a dead end!

Northeast Fourth Company Commander 192

— Zhang Henshui

Chapter 14: Conferring Marriage is Difficult, Hesitating and Worrying About the Future. Inviting Friends to a Small Gathering to Observe the Shameless Past

After reading it, Zhao Ziqiang said: Old Guan, you are really unreasonable. How come you haven't been back for half a month? There are rules in the military camp that you should go home twice a week. You have a family but don't care about it, and you have time but don't go. It's unreasonable. Guan Yaowu said: It's not unreasonable at all. Think about it, the days are still short now. Leaving the camp at six o'clock, I have to run with my legs open to catch up with getting into the city. That's all. Going back to the camp at six o'clock the next day, how can that be done? It's not even dawn yet. Zhao Ziqiang said: Can't you bring your family to Haidian? Guan Yaowu shook his head and said: I simply don't want to go home. What's the point of bringing my family here? Going back is the wife nagging, the children吵闹, and it makes me feel irritable. It's better to just mess around in the camp. My family now, including adults and children, needs a total of forty or fifty yuan a month to get by. Think about it, the salary can't be paid monthly, and I have to take out this much money a month. How much money can I spend myself? This family is really exhausting me. Zhao Ziqiang said: Since you don't love your family that much, why are you so enthusiastic about setting me up with a match? Guan Yaowu laughed and said: What am I enthusiastic about? Didn't you come to me time and time again to persuade me? The inspection committee is coming soon, let's go. As he said this, he sighed and went downstairs. Zhao Ziqiang was disappointed and somewhat lost, and had to go back to his company. The inspection lasted for a total of seven days, and today was the last day of the hygiene inspection. The inspection committee arrived at Zhao's company, took a look, saw the bedding on the floor covered with snow-white cloth, the toilets lined with snow-white lime, and yellow soil sprinkled on the sidewalks. Their faces showed a happy expression, and they left. Zhao Ziqiang thought that he had been busy for half a month: it was all for this half-hour of showiness. Thinking about it, it's really boring. Even someone like Guan Yaowu, who is unwilling to spend money, also took out the money from his pocket to pad the expenses. It can be seen that this idea of ​​being competitive is something that no one can break. (172)

World Oddities

— Chu Yu

Traveling Around Europe by Boat 193

Two German teenagers, Tai Ulrek and Xiusuozhi'ai, traveled around Europe in a small boat only twenty feet long, starting from the docks of Hamburg. The two teenagers set off from Hamburg in March of the year before last, reached Copenhagen, the capital of Denmark, went through the Baltic Sea to Leningrad, then went up the Volga Canal in the upper reaches to Russia, then out of the Black Sea until January of this year, reached the port of Senoa in Italy, then crossed the Mediterranean Sea, cruised the seaports of Spain and Portugal, crossed the Bay of Biscay, the English Channel, and returned to Hamburg. This adventurous small boat trip really makes us extremely admire them.

One Person with Two Hearts 194

An American named Edward Leinuoluoshi from Bizhizhiba is thirty-two years old this year. He was diagnosed at a clinic, and the doctor was greatly surprised when he shone an X-ray on him, because he had two hearts, one on the right side, like an ordinary heart, and another heart on the left side, which was smaller.

Drinks of People from Different Countries 195

If we go to Paris, France in the summer, we can see the various drinks of people from different countries. For example, if French and German people are thirsty, they like to drink beer with a little alcohol the most, so their tables are full of beer bottles. British people like to drink warm tea, Spanish and South American people only drink warm coffee, and Americans especially like to drink iced tea and iced coffee, and often add lemon juice, orange juice, etc. This is probably because people from different countries have different preferences.

Descendants of Persia Return Home 196

Twenty wealthy men in India, whose combined assets amount to 350 million yuan, have been selected by the Persian government to promote the prosperity of Persia, and have been invited to return home. The Persian government has selected a thousand square miles of land to accommodate the ancient Persian Zoroastrians living in India. It is said that the ancestors of these Indians were exiled from Persia to India 1,200 years ago, and their descendants made a fortune in India and finally returned to their hometown.

Giant Dolphin 197

Recently, a fisherman named Gebala from the island of Kouba in the West Indies caught a sea hog that was six meters and twenty-one feet long and weighed a thousand pounds. It was a rare and unheard-of giant sea hog. Later, when a bullock cart was used to move it ashore, it could not be hoisted. It took two or three cranes to move the monster ashore.

Gold in the Human Body 198

A miner at the Yohanasbuolok gold mine in South Africa worked in the gold mine for twenty years. After he took a bath in a bathtub, twenty ounces of pure gold, worth 420 yuan, settled at the bottom of the bathtub the next morning. Many other miners in the same mine also had a lot of gold sticking to their bodies, which settled at the bottom of the tub after they took a bath. Therefore, people call them golden bodies.

A Sea Leopard Worth 50,000 Yuan 199

The Berlin Zoo in Germany has more than 800 species of birds and more than 500 species of mammals, totaling more than 4,000 birds and animals, surpassing the London Zoo. Among these 4,000 animals, the most precious is the giant sea leopard produced in Antarctica, worth 45,000 yuan, weighing 4,500 pounds, and eating about 160 pounds of fish every day.

The World's Casino 200

The world-famous Monte Carlo Casino, which has been open since 1862, has declared its closure due to the world's economic panic. It is said that in the past two or three years, gamblers have rarely come in winter, and income has plummeted, while expenses are at least 50,000 to 60,000 yuan per day. Recently, under the guise of cleaning, part of the casino has been converted into a sports ground, leaving only a small part to barely maintain its appearance.

Fish Can Deliver Mail 201

The strange tale of diamonds in the belly of a fish has been generally recognized by society. Recently, there has been a strange story that fish can deliver mail. When a Dutch postal worker was passing through the Hagge fish market, he saw a fish seller cut open a fish and take out a letter from the fish's belly. The address and name on the letter were very clear. It was sent from Norway. However, many people thought that a sailor accidentally dropped the letter into the sea, and it was swallowed by a fish. Coincidentally, the fish swam to the Dutch border and was caught.

Economic Society Annual Meeting 203

Re-election of Directors and Determination of the Location of the Next Annual Meeting

Shen Honglie's Reception and Tour of Famous Attractions

丨Members from Qingdao to Jinan丨

(Qingdao, 28th) All members of the Economic Society left Qingdao for Jinan at 7:00 AM on the 28th. Peng Xuepei left earlier last night due to official business. Naini Guang and Zhou Zuomin stayed in Qingdao due to business matters. President Ma Yinchu said that he was very impressed with Qingdao's construction achievements and was especially grateful for the thoughtful hospitality. (Jinan, 28th) Members of the Chinese Economic Society, including Ma Yinchu and Chen Qicai, arrived in Jinan with more than 50 people. Han, the head of the Finance Department, and the Mayor of Jinan went to the station to greet and welcome them. Ma and Chen got off the car to visit Han. Chen will return to Beijing tonight. Ma and others are scheduled to visit Mount Tai on the 29th and then return south. Two public associations and the provincial government will host banquets in stages. The 10th Annual Meeting of the Chinese Economic Society was held at 2:00 PM on August 26 at the Science Museum of Shandong University. Li Quanshi presided over the meeting. Secretary Xu Zhaosun, Accountant Xu Jilian, and Foundation Accountant Wang Guanghua (represented by Xu Zhaosun) successively reported the general situation of the past year. It was resolved that the ordinary accounting should be reviewed by Wu Shirui, and the foundation accounting should be reviewed by Pan Xulun. Next, Li Quanshi reported on the expenses and editorial affairs of the Economic Quarterly. It was resolved that the expenses of the Quarterly should be reviewed by Liu Dajun.

Re-election of Directors: The society has a total of nine directors, and one-third are re-elected each year. The three whose terms expired this year were Jia Shiyi, Zhang Gongquan, and Li Zhaohuan. Liu Tingmian was appointed by the chairman to call the votes, and Wu Yugan and Yang Yinpu recorded the votes. As a result of the vote, Li Zhaohuan, Wang Yunwu, and Jin Guobao were elected as directors. Yang Yinpu, Tang Qingzeng, and Zhou Zuomin, who received the next most votes, were elected as alternate directors.

Location of the Next Annual Meeting: The locations for the 11th Annual Meeting next year were determined to be Chongqing, Wenzhou, and Beijing. The board of directors will select one of them to hold the meeting at that time. The meeting adjourned at around 4:00 PM.

Shen's Reception: At noon on the 26th, various Qingdao agencies, the Jiaoji Railway Bureau, the Qingdao Customs, the Unified Tax Bureau, the Salt Affairs Audit Office, etc., jointly hosted a banquet at the Yingbin Hotel. At 7:00 PM, Mayor Shen Honglie hosted a dinner at the Yingbin Hotel. During the dinner, Shen delivered a speech, first stating that Qingdao Port has unique advantages in terms of favorable natural conditions and geographical location, and was only recovered after being managed by Germany and Japan for 20 years. Whether the municipal administration is well-managed is the key to the speed of recovery of other concession areas. Therefore, the development and prosperity of Qingdao should concentrate the talents and financial resources of the entire country to achieve it. Next, he described the recent political and economic construction of Qingdao. Seven construction offices have been set up in the rural areas. The municipal government and various bureaus send people to inspect and investigate each district every week. The work of the staff in each office is mostly to go out to guide farmers in the field. They strive for practicality in their work. In recent years, there has been no separation between the top and bottom levels, and they have learned a lot about the hardships of the people. In terms of economy, the rural land tax revenue is more than 80,000 yuan per year, while the expenses for rural construction and agricultural improvement experiments reach more than 300,000 yuan. Regarding its effectiveness, for example, about 80,000 pear trees were planted in the city. In the past two years, they did not bear fruit due to insect pests. After the government injected pesticides last year, they have borne fruit this year. On average, each tree is worth four yuan, totaling more than 300,000 yuan, which is a small compensation for the farmers. 2. In the urban area, they have recruited leaders and talents from all walks of life to engage in autonomous construction and set up places to accommodate opium addicts, beggars, and petty thieves, so the public security is relatively calm. Citizens can indeed leave their doors unlocked at night. In terms of economy, 180,000 yuan was spent to build the Fifth Wharf, and the old wharves and warehouses were repaired. The land in the factory area is stipulated that only national product factories can buy it. They are doing their best to build Qingdao in terms of both manpower and material resources. However, the matter is of great importance, and it is beyond the ability of one place to handle. They hope that talented and powerful people from all over the country will invest in development. Moreover, the people of our country have very low desires for life and are very耐苦. Generally, they hope to live and work in peace. Although Qingdao is difficult to be called楽業, the people can still安居. At the beginning of my tenure, I vowed not to increase donations and taxes. Since taking office, I have exempted many harsh taxes and miscellaneous taxes that are harmful to the people, and there are absolutely no increases. This can be gratifying. Later, Chen Qicai delivered a speech of thanks, saying that the Qingdao Mayor is indeed doing things for the people alone, which is unprecedented in the country.

Tour and Visit: On the morning of the 27th, the Qingdao Municipal Government hosted a tour of the Licun Model Village and then went to Laoshan for sightseeing. On the morning of the 28th, they took a Jiaoji Railway train to Jinan. On the 29th, they visited famous attractions such as Daming Lake and Baotu Spring, and were entertained by the Shandong Provincial Government and the Jinan Municipality. That night, they went to Tai'an. On the 30th, they visited Mount Tai. That night, they went to Qufu. On the 31st, they visited places such as the Confucius Forest. That night, the Beijing-Shanghai members took the train south.

Social Education Society Annual Meeting 204

First Day Situation

In addition to members of the society, attendees included representatives from the Central Party Headquarters, education bureau representatives from Guangdong, Guangxi, Fujian, and Hebei provinces, Chairman Han's representative, Construction Bureau Chief Zhang Honglie, Provincial Party Committee Zhang Weicun, Education Bureau Chief He Siyuan, and others. A group photo was taken at 8:00 AM, and the meeting commenced at 8:30 AM. Yu Qingtang served as chairman, with Wang Zhang, Rui Lin, Xiao Dichen, and Yu Shigai recording the proceedings in the morning. In the afternoon, Yu Ruming, Fan Yunshi, Yan Zhewu, and Dong Taisheng served as masters of ceremonies, with Zhang Ziyu as the registrar. The ceremonies were conducted as prescribed. Chairman Yu Qingtang delivered the opening address, followed by addresses from Chairman Han's representative Zhang Honglie, Education Bureau Chief He Siyuan representing the Ministry of Education, and Zhao Mian, the director of the board of directors' office, who reported on the society's activities over the past year. Subsequently, guest speakers included Lei Hongkun, representative of the Guangdong Provincial Education Bureau; Zhang Yongrong, representative of the Fujian Education Bureau; Liu Zaizhou, representative of the Shaanxi Education Bureau; Lei Rongyong, representative of the Guangxi Education Bureau; Chen Dongyuan, representative of the Anhui Education Bureau; Zhang Yi and Zhang Hongfu, representatives of the Hebei Education Bureau; Yu Botong, representative of the Shanxi Education Bureau; Chen Guyuan, representative of the Central Party Headquarters; Mr. Wang, representative of the Henan Education Bureau; Sheng Binu, representative of Beiping City; and Su Yunzhi, representative of the First Normal School. These were followed by speeches from Hebei member Li Yi

fei, Jiangsu member Chen Lijiang, Zouping member Yang Xiaochun, Jiangsu member Tai Shuangqiu, Gaoyang, and others. By the time these speeches concluded, it was already 12:00 PM. Chairman Yu Qingtang reported that the original schedule was for speeches to begin at 7:30 AM, but due to the photography, the meeting did not commence until 8:30 AM. He had hoped that representatives from various provinces would provide more guidance, but due to time

constraints, the opening ceremony concluded. He expressed gratitude to the Shandong Provincial Government for its hospitality and to the guests for their participation, and he noted that all members present were paying attention. He also reported that: (1) Mr. Niu Yongjian's scheduled speech was canceled due to Mr. Niu's unavailability. (2) Chairman Han's banquet would be held at 5:00 PM, and he hoped that everyone would attend on time. Additionally, he stated that this afternoon, after the committee meeting, in order to save time, they planned to extend the meeting by twenty or thirty minutes. They would immediately continue with the general assembly to discuss the organization review committee and to nominate and elect directors and ballot counters. This was unanimously approved, and the general assembly was immediately convened, with Peng Baichuan as chairman. The matters discussed included: (1) Organizing four types of review committees. Members could voluntarily join any group by submitting a written request to the presidium, which would then be allocated by the chairman. This was approved. (2) Designating Zhao Qixun and eight others as ballot counters for the afternoon's election of directors, and Kong Jing'an and four others as vote supervisors. This was approved. (3) A proposal by members Yu Qingtang and others to thank the Shandong Provincial Government, the Shandong Education Bureau, and the Shandong Provincial People's Education Hall for their hospitality was approved. (4) A proposal by the board of directors that the representatives attending the annual meeting donate funds to provide relief for the Shandong flood was approved. The board of directors printed donation collection books, and female members present volunteered to collect donations from all members. The meeting adjourned close to 1:00 PM. In the afternoon, groups reviewed the proposals, followed by speeches from Zhang Honglie, representative of the Shandong Provincial Government, and He Siyuan, director of the Central Party Headquarters Education Bureau, as well as speeches from various guests and members. Furthermore, the general assembly received a telegram from Qi Zhenru, director of the Henan Education Bureau, stating that education in Henan Province was backward and requesting that the next annual meeting be held in Henan.

Second Day Situation 205

(Jinan Correspondence) The second annual meeting of the China Social Education Society continued at the Jinan Public Education Hall (on the 25th) at 8:00 AM. One hundred and fourteen members were in attendance, with Dong Huai as chairman and Dong Taisheng, Yan Zhewu, Fan Yunshi, and Yu Ruming recording the proceedings. After the ceremonies were completed, the central issue was discussed, which was the "Revitalization of the Nation through Rural Construction" proposal. Liang Shuming, the original drafter of the first group, explained the proposal in fifty minutes, outlining the first step and the second step. The procedures for discussion were decided as follows: (1) combine all groups for discussion, (2) freely express opinions, (3) each person's speech should not exceed five minutes each time, (4) first discuss the principles, then discuss the steps and methods. The representatives of various provinces hoped that the principles, steps, and methods of this problem would be obtained as reference for promotion in various places, because the bankruptcy of rural China and the crisis of the nation are indeed

urgent needs for salvation, and the debate was extremely fierce. The meeting adjourned at 12:00 PM. The meeting resumed at 2:00 PM in the afternoon, with Gao Yang as chairman. According to the resolutions of the morning, the discussions were carried out. When discussing the theory, Liang Shuming's draft was used as the center, and other proposals were also merged for discussion. Various theoretical questions about rural construction were elaborated in detail. Later, the method issue was discussed. In addition to discussing specific facilities, the new social organization in Liang Shuming's proposal was discussed in detail. In the end, it was decided that the "Revitalization of the Nation through Rural Construction" proposal should first be reviewed by the review committee, and then submitted to the general assembly. The general assembly recommended seven people: Lei Hongkun, Zhao Mian, Shuangqiu, Yu Qingtang, Dong Huai, Liang Shuming, and Chen Li. The board of directors selected Gao Yang, Zhao Jiliang, and Tang Xianzhi as review committee members, and the review was scheduled to begin at 6:00 PM that evening.

Dong Huai, the director of the Provincial Public Education Hall, and Yang Zhanyun, the chief of the third section of the Education Bureau, hosted a banquet for all members and held an entertainment event at the Public Education Hall to add to the fun. In addition, the five members of the society's board of directors had reached the end of their terms. According to the regulations, one person should be re-appointed by the board of directors, and the other four should be elected by the general assembly. The voting and election took place yesterday, and the results of the ballot count were announced today. Chen Lijiang, Dong Renjian, Peng Baichuan, and Shang Zhongyi were elected.

Annual Meeting of the China Library Association

Proposal for Circulation Library of Shen Bao 208

Use Postal Delivery to Deepen the Circulation of Books into Rural Areas

Compile "Reading Guidance" to Guide Out-of-School Youths

The Circulation Library of Shen Bao has been established for less than a year, and it has spared no effort in supporting social and cultural undertakings, so the results are remarkable, and it is praised by the people of this city. The China Library Association is holding its second annual meeting in Beiping. Based on the previous experience of the library, it believes that the most urgent task to be carried out now is to submit the following two proposals to the association. The reporter found the original manuscript and quickly recorded it here.

(1) Library undertakings should be actively promoted to popularize them in townships and towns in the shortest possible time.

A. Reasons: There are three instruments for promoting culture today: newspapers, magazines, and books. There are two tools for promoting them: schools and libraries. However, the nature of libraries is different from that of schools. The purpose of schools is to cultivate talents, and the mission is to enlighten and instruct. Except for the enlightenment and instruction, other research is not involved, and those who are economically distressed are not involved. Libraries are different. Regardless of wealth or poverty, regardless of class, they uniformly provide the intelligence and opinions needed. This is what is meant by "education without discrimination." This is known to everyone. However, there are more libraries in cities, the facilities are more complete, and the collection of books is more abundant. As for smaller county towns, due to financial constraints, even if there are any, there are only one or two, and the facilities are inevitably simple and crude. As for the towns, it is difficult to find one or two out of thousands, let alone the countryside. This is not because people in rural towns cannot read, nor is it because people in rural towns do not like to read. It is simply because there are no such cultural institutions in remote areas. Our country is based on agriculture, and although there are no accurate statistics on the population of rural areas and cities, the ratio is roughly seven to three. Therefore, promoting rural education should be more important than urban education. In recent years, people who are concerned about the times have shouted the slogan "Go to the countryside," the calls are getting louder, the publicity is getting wider, and the promotion is sparing no effort. However, farmers are limited in their knowledge, and many still superstitiously believe in the authority of gods. Common sense is lacking and reason is blocked. Even if we want to reform them, they are used to their old habits, and the effect is very small. Therefore, popular books can circulate in townships and towns, so that their erroneous views can be subtly changed, and then given appropriate guidance, they will not be resisted. This move can create a large number of soldiers among the farmers themselves, which is especially important, and the progress of the country also relies on it. B. Methods: (1) In addition to the existing public and private libraries, establish book circulation points in each district and township, attached to the district office and other public places, which should be equipped with newspapers, magazines, and popular books, etc., for the exclusive use of township and town residents and farmers to come to the society or borrow back for reading. This method should be submitted to the Ministry of Education to order the education bureaus of each county to organize it in a unified manner, so that it can be implemented conveniently and easily achieve practical results. The above method is time-consuming and will definitely not be completed in a short period of time. Before the establishment of libraries in various rural districts, postal delivery can be used. If it can be handled perfectly, then wherever the postal route reaches, the library undertaking will be promoted, and the effect will be very great. At the same time, it should be presented to the Ministry of Education and the Ministry of Transportation in the name of the National Library to order the national post office to provide various conveniences for any library to send or return books, and the postage should also be reduced to the greatest extent. It concerns the promotion of culture and education, and the authorities will surely approve it. Regarding postal book delivery, it is said that the Zhejiang Private Circulation Library has already implemented it. This library is currently in the trial stage in this city. (3) If this method is agreed upon and happily adopted by libraries across the country, then there is a further method that can divide national libraries into several regions according to the number of books in the collection, the convenience of transportation, and the distance from the location. Within each region, designate one or several libraries to be used exclusively by any public in that region. As for the regulations, deadlines, guarantees, etc., they can be determined separately according to the local environment and different situations. (4) If a book is unique to a library in one region and another region needs to read it, it can be borrowed from each other in the name of the library. If it is a rare or out-of-print edition, a copy can be made to respond to it. If the above method is put into practice, then even in places where the atmosphere is closed, one can enjoy the ointment of knowledge. Compared with the patrol book cart, which only facilitates readers in nearby areas, its significance is extraordinary. Is it appropriate, please wait for public decision.

(2) Libraries should jointly compile "Reading Guidance" as a criterion for readers.

A. Reasons: Ancient and modern classics are vast like the sea. Since the European winds have gradually moved eastward, scholars have been diligently studying Eastern and Western academics, so there are more and more writings and translations are constantly emerging. Beginners, although they are determined to study a certain discipline, have a feeling of being at a loss. In the end, blind people and blind horses pick up at will, and once they encounter a setback, they abandon it immediately and change to another discipline, and so on. Is it not a great pity that there are those who do not succeed in their lives? However, if you want to correct this shortcoming, you can only compile "Reading Guidance", from shallow to deep, step by step, so that readers can follow it and not waste time. However, this matter is of great importance, and no one can be competent without special expertise, because every word and sentence is of great importance to the reader, so it cannot be done hastily. B. Methods: (1) Elect specialists from among the members to take on difficult tasks. Those who are good at social sciences will be assigned to social sciences, and those who are good at natural sciences will be asked to take on natural sciences. (2) If there is a lack of such talent among the members, hire experts with advanced knowledge to take on the task. (3) The arrangement of "Reading Guidance" must be divided into two categories: "required reading" and "reference." Each category is divided into several subjects, and the arrangement of book titles for each subject must be from shallow to deep. Each book title must be accompanied by a concise summary. The book titles listed in this "Reading Guidance" should be the essential books, and libraries across the country should have one or several copies prepared for readers to read. If it can be compiled properly, then readers will be like sailing the sea and getting a compass, and reading each book can be done with half the effort and twice the result. Is it appropriate, please wait for public decision.

High School or Above

Buglers Should Be Set Up to Benefit Military Training 209

The Municipal Education Bureau Ordered All Schools to Comply

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau instructed the middle schools in this city that the Ministry of Education instructed in its No. 700 order, "According to the report from the military instructors of various schools, the bugle sound is also a kind of education, so students often urge and use buglers, but because the plan does not have this provision, most schools seem to be missing it. It is proposed to order the setting up of buglers to benefit military training." It is said that the use of bugle sound is originally to regulate advances and retreats, discipline, neat steps, uniform work and rest, and maintain the order of the entire army at ordinary times. It represents the transmission of orders in battle, so it occupies an important position in the military organization. Now that military education has been implemented in high schools and above, military courses should uniformly use bugle sound so that students have a common sense of bugle sound, and the equipment of buglers is indispensable. According to the previous situation, we should consult and ask you to inform all high schools and above to comply. At least one bugler must be set up in each school (in addition to blowing the bugle sound, the bugler is also responsible for cleaning and keeping weapons and performing various duties with the military instructor) to benefit military training and hope to see changes. Furthermore, if all work and rest in the school can uniformly use the bugle sound to cultivate students' military life, it would be even more appropriate. Please also inform, etc." According to this, it is found that the bugle sound is a kind of military education, so that students can understand the bugle sound. Each school can add a bugler to play the bugle and be responsible for all duties in military training. In addition to consulting and replying and issuing orders, it is ordered that the bureau instruct the public and private high schools and above under its jurisdiction to handle the matter as appropriate, etc. The third batch.

British Wimbledon

World Tennis Conference Diary (6) 217

London Special Correspondence: A Record

Tuesday (July 4th) 218

Today's temperature is even higher, reaching 85 degrees, the air is dry, with little moisture. Today's matches were relatively less important, and the audience dwindled from its peak, all preparing to return on Wednesday to watch the men's singles quarterfinals and other crucial matches. The first match did not finish until 8:30 PM. The central court was only half full after half a day of matches, yet there were still many empty seats.

Thanks to Ms. Round's victory, England gained a position in the women's singles quarterfinals. Her opponent was Ms. Van Leo, who succumbed in two sets, winning only five games in total. However, the situation wasn't so straightforward. Round seemed unhappy in the first set, until the Italian woman took a 3-1 lead, after which Round rallied, making it 5-3 and then 6-3. Round's shots lacked power and were too soft, allowing her opponent to often answer and return the best shots. Once Round took the lead, she suddenly perked up and gave it her all. Ms. Van Leo's shots were heavy and powerful but not practical. Round gritted her teeth and proved even better than Van Leo.

The match between Ms. Jacobs and Mrs. Mathieu on the central court was a feast of excellent tennis skills for the audience. Jacobs won the first set 6-1, and then Mrs. Mathieu responded in kind. This match was a struggle between chops and drives. Jacobs took a more offensive approach, using serves, volleys, and smashes to counter Mathieu's baseline drives. After Mrs. Mathieu got the ball with her forehand, her returns were so skillful, almost on par with men's tennis. The ball traveled straight and fast. Although Mathieu didn't often approach the net, she could also smash. Although both the first and second sets were one-sided, the competition was fierce. If there was an opening, they would immediately seize it to attack. In the third set, both players performed very well. Jacobs broke serve, taking a 2-0 lead. Such winning serves were commonplace and not considered too much. Once, Jacobs missed an easy smash, almost causing disaster, but she rallied and broke her opponent's serve again, making it 4-2. In the end, Mathieu failed with a double fault on her serve. The result of the match was as it should be; Jacobs was fresher and made almost no mistakes. Such thoughtful play, even from a woman, should be commended.

England's most promising female tennis player, Ms. Round, wins a spot in the Wimbledon singles final.

The match between Ms. Krawinkel and Ms. Skreven followed, but the level of play was noticeably lower, by nine-tenths. Both sides stood at the backcourt and drove the ball. Initially, it was interesting, but it later became monotonous. Skreven's forehand drive was her distinguishing feature. Apart from her powerful drive, which was often followed by approaching the net and scoring, there was little else commendable. Krawinkel's valuable experience gave her a significant advantage. In the first two sets, the scores were even. Skreven was at her peak during her final period of victory, running swiftly and reacting quickly. Her shots spun over the net. Apart from her forehand drive and the occasional smash, Skreven lacked training in other types of shots, which was truly a pity.

The men's doubles matches were numerous, bizarre, and unpredictable. Pan-Ly-Hughs lost to Bowers-Shang-Si-Yang in five sets. Seeder-Stauffen suffered the same fate against Oliver and Hake-Lof-Totte. The two matches were held simultaneously, one on the central court and one on the first court. Bowers was the best of the four. Hughs-Shang-Si-Yang was weak and prone to errors, as was Pan-Ly. The English team was eliminated in the fifth set, losing 6-4.

Seeder-Stauffen lost the first two sets consecutively, the second set by 6-2. After that, all their efforts were in vain. Seeder was poor in all aspects for the most part, and although he exerted himself with all his strength, his judgment was a major flaw, and he lacked creativity. Stauffen was better, but on Stauffen's side, many line calls were incorrect. Oliver deserves the most credit, leading his partner and never being frustrated or disappointed. Hake-Lof-Totte was a tall and energetic Englishman who was lackluster in the first two sets but gradually improved later, often seen hitting the ball hard. The two Americans did not surrender easily, especially in the fourth set, with a score of 9-11. Once, Stauffen missed a shot and, turning around, threw his racket at the net. The racket tumbled across the ground for over twenty feet.

The second match scheduled was Thorm-Bill-Quist-Totte against Ander-Lay-Strandt-man, the conquerors of Van-Nes-Gran-Hill. They won the last two sets consecutively, making it very pleasant. Baugh-Lo-Ku-La-Bul-Lu-Ning's match against Crawford-Mack-Gray-Siss took place after 7 o'clock, with the outcome decided in four sets. Although Baugh was not very good, he managed to maintain his advantage. Baugh's support of Bul-Lu-Ning was greatly applauded, and his shots were superb. Overall, the French team will still retain the championship. Mack-Gray-Siss was completely useless except for the third set. On the court, he seemed confused. The ratio of Crawford's good shots to bad shots was about three to one, but Crawford ultimately could not bear the entire burden.

Sato and Van-Nes were guests at this match. From now on, Sato will surely know what Crawford is like.
