Co-authored by Wu Yunrui and Yuan Dunli

"Principles of Physical Education" Published Today 220

A Monumental Work in the Field of Physical Education

Everything in the universe has principles. If we follow these principles, we can achieve twice the result with half the effort. If we go against them, our efforts will be in vain. Physical education certainly has its underlying principles. The Diligence Bookstore at 392 Rue Pére Robert, French Concession, Shanghai, recognizing this, has specially commissioned Wu Yunrui, Director of the Department of Physical Education at National Central University, and Yuan Dunli, Director of the Department of Physical Education at Peiping Normal University, to co-author the book "Principles of Physical Education," which has now been published. The richness of the material gathered and the accuracy of the citations are unlike ordinary works. It can be considered the most successful and elaborate masterpiece in the field of physical education in China. The book is divided into nine major chapters, each further divided into sections: Chapter 1, Introduction; Section 1, What are Principles; Section 2, The Importance of Physical Education Principles; Section 3, The Source of Physical Education Principles; Section 4, The Meaning of Physical Education. Chapter 2, Historical Background; Section 1, The Meaning of History and its Analysis; Section 2, The Importance of Studying Historical Backgrounds; Section 3, The Background of Physical Education in Germany; Section 4, The Background of Physical Education in Sweden; Section 5, The Background of Physical Education in France; Section 6, The Background of Physical Education in England; Section 7, The Background of Physical Education in the United States; Section 8, The Background of Physical Education in China. Chapter 3, Social Background; Section 1, Social Evolution and Physical Education; Section 2, Political Conditions and Physical Education; Section 3, How Physical Education Promotes Social Progress. Chapter 4, The Relationship Between Mind and Body and Physical Education; Section 1, Introduction; Section 2, Dualism of Mind and Body; Section 3, Monism of Mind and Body; Section 4, The Mind-Body Problem and Physical Education. Chapter 5, The Nature of Man and Physical Education; Section 1, The Biological Basis of Life; Section 2, Primitive Activities of Mankind; Section 3, The Facts of Human Development; Section 4, Growth and Development; Section 5, The Influence of Physical Education on Physical Development; Section 6, The Meaning of Instinct; Section 7, The Nature of Sex; Section 8, The Transfer of Training. Chapter 6, The Purpose of Physical Education; Section 1, Investigation of the Purpose of Physical Education; Section 2, Analysis of the Purpose of Physical Education; Section 3, The Purpose Achieved by Various Activities in Physical Education. Chapter 7, Opposing Views on Physical Education; Section 1, Taoist Naturalism or Non-Actionism versus Legalist Rule of Law; Section 2, Utilitarianism and Culturalism and Physical Education; Section 3, Interestism and Effortism. Chapter 8, Physical Education and Education; Section 1, The Evolution of the Relationship Between Physical Education and Education; Section 2, The Inseparability of Physical Education and Education; Section 3, The Educational Value of Physical Education; Section 4, The Contribution of Physical Education to Improving Practical Education; Section 5, The Position of Physical Education in Education. Chapter 9, The Relationship Between Physical Education and Other Activities; Section 1, Physical Education and Health Education; Section 2, Physical Education and Military Training; Section 3, Physical Education and Boy Scouts; Section 4, Physical Education and National Martial Arts. The book is in 24mo format, finely printed on 100-pound woodfree paper, with beautiful and elegant binding, available in hardcover and paperback. The hardcover is priced at $2.20 (silver dollars) per copy, and the paperback is priced at $1.60 (silver dollars) per copy, with a special 10% discount. The bookstore's storefront at 554 4th Avenue, British Concession, is also selling the book at the same time.

Page 17

Free Talk

Ode to Sleep Sickness 226

— Wen

Recently, I heard that a type of sleep sickness is prevalent in America, spreading rampantly. Although I don't quite understand the symptoms, judging from the name of the disease, I find it to be a rather delightful ailment.

First, if the germs that cause this illness, similar to a fever, are researched and neutralized appropriately for injection, then those suffering from insomnia will no longer have to worry about not being able to sleep.

Second, for those who are afraid of their wives, who can't get things done, who suffer from seasickness, or who encounter misfortune, wanting a temporary reprieve, they can also enjoy the pleasure of sound sleep. The ideal in the famous short story "Rip Van Winkle" by American author Washington Irving can now be effortlessly realized, wouldn't that be a joyous thing?

However, people's fear of this sleep sickness seems to stem from the fear of falling asleep and never waking up. This, I think, is just a shortsighted view stemming from a lack of foresight. To those who can see things clearly, there is no significant difference between a long sleep and a short nap. For example, our modern-day compatriots in Greater China, who are immersed in opium and gambling, in fine wine and women, in money, power, and status, once they become addicted, when will they ever wake up?

The summer holidays are over, and the cool season of early autumn is approaching. I hope that all my compatriots, both high and low, who are enthusiastic about fame and fortune, competing in the martial arts and literary circles, can seek out some sleep sickness germs to enjoy a good sleep and rest. This is much simpler and more convenient than going all the way to Lushan Mountain or spending lavishly in Qingdao to escape the summer heat.

Eventful July 227

— Lin Yizhi

Seeing Mr. Jianwen's "Random Talk about July," which lists the past events of the Double Seventh Festival, Bon Odori, etc., I can't help but feel nostalgic; but past events are just past events, after all, not reality. Looking back at the reality of July, it still makes people frown. Living in a lane house in Shanghai, it is impossible to see how the Cowherd and Weaver Girl are whispering sweet nothings beside the Milky Way, and the modern girls sweating beside the machines, struggling for a few dimes of wages, are of course even more unable to ask for skill. The rich and powerful men on the street are organizing temple fairs, holding a donation book and going door-to-door to solicit donations. The momentum is almost the same as the apportionment of military expenses in the countryside. It's really not a joyous festival. When I was a child, I heard adults say that in the seventh month of the lunar calendar, the King of Hell would show great kindness and release all the little ghosts locked in the eighteen layers of hell, allowing them to stir up trouble in the human world. Especially those who died violently would take this opportunity to look for a scapegoat, so July is an ominous month, often with rampant epidemics and widespread deaths. When the lives of ordinary people are suddenly invaded, they can only show no resistance and prepare good wine and meat to treat them, hoping to reduce some disasters, which is the purpose of holding the Ullambana Festival. The impermanent scolding of dogs in the Ullambana Festival was my favorite thing to listen to when I was a child. It is said that evil ghosts are afraid of impermanence. Although impermanence is scolding dogs, evil ghosts will also avoid it when they hear it. But in our current era, although the human world is so chaotic, the King of Hell in the underworld seems to be holding on to a consistent policy of laissez-faire, not only in July, but actually releasing those five funeral evil ghosts all year round to run rampant everywhere in the human world, causing unbearable disturbances. The common people are providing them with even the last drop of blood and flesh. The Ullambana Festival has been held countless times, but impermanence and evil ghosts are of the same kind, and they only know how to eat the good wine and meat of the common people.

Regarding July, my hometown also has a saying:

"Worrying day and night, especially worrying about the fifth watch of July 23rd."

This is because storms and floods are prone to occur in July, and it is said that the fifth watch of July 23rd is the moment to determine the good or bad fortune of the year. This year, the Yellow River has already breached its banks, and there are already major floods in Shandong and Jiangbei; in the rural areas of Jiangsu and Zhejiang, there are droughts and locust plagues. The good or bad luck of the year does not need to be predicted at the fifth watch of July 23rd.

From this point of view, July is still an eventful month. However, according to the elders, on July 30th, the Ksitigarbha Bodhisattva opens his eyes, and the little ghosts must from then on restrain their tracks, and the osmanthus blooms in August, with clear skies and refreshing air, there should be a different scene. Then, let's wait for this "July 30th."

At Dusk 228

— Kang De

As twilight silently rises, the pedestrians on the street, who were originally leisurely strolling, become a bit scattered: they are going back to their homes to rest.

I first look at the much quieter street, then slowly wander a few steps, following the flight path of the tired birds returning to their nests, back to my lodging. The lodging is in a small alley at the end of a secluded lane. The room is not very small, but it is as dilapidated as a withered temple.

Few people walk down the secluded lane, and in the small alley, apart from the rustling sound of fallen leaves, there is only the frantic barking of stray dogs crouching in the darkness upon hearing the sound of footsteps. This sudden, unprovoked barking of stray dogs always makes me feel uneasy. I originally tried to lighten my footsteps when walking into the alley, and walked quickly: but the dog's hearing is as sensitive as its sense of smell. I thought I was walking so lightly that there was no sound, but it still suddenly barked, so I lost the ability to lighten my footsteps, and instead ran wildly with big strides, and it barked even more fiercely. I would still feel my heart pounding until I walked straight into the room and closed the door.

The landlord's family had already eaten dinner and were gathered under the lamp, chatting about everyday life with their children and daughters-in-law. The children, chirping and singing like little birds, would call out "Uncle, uncle" when they heard footsteps, followed by the landlord's kind "You're back, haven't you eaten yet?"

I mumbled a response, walked into the pitch-black room, and first fumbled for the matches I had forgotten where I had put them; after much bumping and stumbling, I finally found them. After lighting them, I shone them on the oil lamp, and I could see that only a dead snake-like wick was lying stiffly inside the transparent lamp belly. The oil was gone. A wave of irrepressible annoyance washed over me, and I stared blankly at the oil-less lampstand until the embers of the match burned my fingertips. I threw away the matchstick and sat silently in the darkness, the sound of the evening wind outside seemed to be blowing on my heart.

"The kerosene is gone, right? Come over here and take some to use."

The landlord's words were carried over with the sound of opening the long window. I politely declined her kindness, and immediately fumbled for the kerosene bottle and hurried out with my head down. I was afraid that if I sat there any longer, the tear stains on my cheeks would fall into her eyes.

The night wind was so cool, and the clothes on my body were so thin. I walked with my hands clasped in my sleeves, holding the kerosene bottle, only my own thin shadow under the dim streetlights accompanying me.

My body and heart were trembling a little.

The Embryo of Ma Zhiyuan's Zaju 229

— Zhao Jingshen

Ma Zhiyuan was one of the most prominent literati of the Yuan Dynasty, with both Zaju and Sanqu being called unparalleled. I believe that his Zaju, such as "Breaking the Dream of the Lone Goose, Autumn in the Han Palace," (the above two dramas are found in the Yuanqu Xuan) "Liu Chen and Ruan Zhao Mistakenly Entered Peach Blossom Spring," (a fragment is recorded in the Northern Lyrics Guangzheng Spectrum, etc.) and "Meng Haoran Walking in the Snow to Seek Plum Blossoms," etc., already had embryos when he composed the Xiaoling. Here are the Xiaoling related to these four dramas:

(1) Meng Qingyang, why so exuberant, riding a donkey frozen on the Ba Bridge. Even if there are some plum blossoms entering the dream, it is not as good as the wind and snow melting the golden tent, slowly sipping and softly singing. (Bo Buduan) (Tune title)

(2) Herb-collecting boy, riding a phoenix guest, resentful of Liu Lang leaving Tiantai. When will the spring breeze come again? The peach blossoms bloom but cannot be eaten, poor scholar with a thin life, who told you to return? (Four Pieces of Jade, Tiantai Road)

(3) Geese flying north, people looking north, abandoning the beautiful Mingfei, the Han emperor and the Xiongnu singing, green grass, is thinking of hometown! (Four Pieces of Jade, Zizhi Road)

(4) Seeing off guests, autumn red cold, singing girl pipa heartbroken. Do you know that Sima listened with sorrow. The moon is bright again, the wine is awake again, the guests just woke up. (Four Pieces of Jade, Xunyang River)

The first song above is the embryo of "Walking in the Snow to Seek Plum Blossoms," the second song is the embryo of "Mistakenly Entered Peach Blossom Spring," the third song is the embryo of "Autumn in the Han Palace," and the fourth song is the embryo of "Qingshan Lei."

The play "Qingshan Lei" shows great respect for Meng Haoran, saying "Meng Haoran is a guest on the Ba Bridge, seeking plum blossoms in the snow" (first act, Jin Zhan'er), and also saying "his poems surpass Meng Haoran" (second act, Tang Xiucai). Perhaps the play "Walking in the Snow to Seek Plum Blossoms" had already been inspired at this time? As for Meng Haoran dying in 740, and Bai Juyi being born thirty-two years later, why should they be blamed for talking together in the same hall? That can be ignored, because a play is ultimately a play, otherwise, unrelated prostitutes would not have been lovers before Bai Juyi. The plot of a prostitute marrying a tea merchant and the moonlit night weeping with the pipa is very similar to "Shuang Jian Ganting Suqing," perhaps influenced by this story to some extent, which is also unknown.

Women (5) 230

— Shen Congwen

She smiled as she looked at the fog. She remembered the thin web of worldly affairs that covered her heart. Yesterday at dusk, she had sat with a female companion on a rock by the sea, listening to the murmur of the waves. One wave after another crashed beneath the rocks. The girl was only seventeen years old and in love with the son of a pastor. The pastor's son, however, thought of her as just a child, and all her plans were based on childish confusion and naivety, bearing no resemblance to what reality would allow. The pastor's son had hurt her heart. She recounted everything, saying that if he continued to treat her like a child, she would prepare to kill herself to show him. She asked the girl, "If you kill yourself, will he understand? Besides suicide, is there no other way to make him understand? And is it even real love? Even if your love for him is genuine, what good qualities does this person actually have?" The girl remained silent for a long time, then raised her head with a shy look and replied, "I don't even know what's going on myself. All his good qualities seem to be found in the character of other boys, but my love for him seems to be solely for that part of his pride where he ignores me. I love that bit of pride." At the time, she thought this girl was truly a child.

But now she had an opportunity for reflection. She did not understand the girl's feelings, and now she was trying her best to seek out the starting and ending points of these feelings.

Too many people loved her, but she did not love them. She felt that all love was very ordinary, and many people seemed both pitiful and laughable in her presence. Many people had altered their souls, emotions, words, and actions, some kind of fixed pattern, because of their love for her. Like a great wind, all kinds of grasses and trees swayed in this wind, and under the storm, no grass or tree could stand firm and still, without wavering at all. Her beauty was also like a great wind. But what she hoped for was a great tree that would never waver, standing proudly before her, not to be conquered by that bit of her beauty. She was looking for this kind of tree, but she had never found it.

She thought, "There won't be this kind of tree by the sea. If I need this kind of tree, I should look for it in the deep mountains."

Indeed, the souls of urban dwellers are all assimilated by an urban education and urban tastes. The souls of all women are cast from one

mold, and the souls of all men are cast from another mold. Individuality and uniqueness are not easy to exist. The leader's standard is produced in a commonly understood example. Everything seems vulgar and ordinary, and everything is transformed into a commodity form. Even human love, the concept before love, and the planning when in love are being turned over in the hands of merchants, all in the same pattern, without any surprises.

There is not a single slightly outstanding tree by the sea. Nor is there a single slightly outstanding person. Although many people fell for her, they all revealed foolishness and did the same things under the same circumstances. Those who were more sophisticated would first use some other reason to be together, and then lose their human form, turning into a dog. Those who were younger would only know how to write the kind of crude and clumsy letters, being humble and flattering in love, pretending. Seeing the foolishness of their own actions, they still could not move the woman. Not knowing how to improve their methods, they would make even more ridiculous expressions, either wanting to commit suicide or saying, "Please be careful," and so on. All love was either extremely foolish or extremely vulgar, so she saw these loves as worthless.

There was really not a single slightly lovable man.

She was tired of those men who had become formulas and the love that had become a formula. She suddenly thought of the pastor's son in the girl's words. She was attracted by a certain curiosity that came and went quickly, and she was a little surprised. She looked at the sky, and a shooting star was streaking across it, so she said to herself softly, "What has passed is over."

But that shooting star in her memory was still flashing with pleasing brilliance. "Only by being stronger can there be brilliance!" She smiled, because she felt that she was extremely strong. However, outside of her consciousness, there lurked a desire, this desire was hidden and the direction was vague.

In one of his novels, Zola mentioned a chaste woman who refused all the flattering and sincere young gentlemen who offered themselves to her.

士,逃到一個小鄕村後,却坦然儘一個粗鹵的農夫,在胃昧中吻了她的嘴唇同手足。驕傲的婦人厭 　輕視了一切柔情,却能在强暴中得到快感。

Zola, after fleeing to a small village, frankly allowed a crude farmer to kiss her lips and limbs in the dark. The proud woman hated and despised all tenderness, but could find pleasure in violence.

She remembered Zola's novel. What she could not understand in that work before, she now fully understood. If there were such a coincidental

encounter, she would, as the story said, "lie down on that golden stack of straw without any refusal." Solid heat, crazy love, the flame burned itself to death and also burned another to death. Only this kind of love is true love!

Tea Market Shows Signs of Development 257

The Soviet Union's Tea Assistance Association has informed various tea merchants regarding various types of black tea from Qimen, Ningzhou, and the two Huguang provinces, as well as Gongxi green tea from Tunxi, Wuyuan, and other areas, that they must all provide new samples for brewing and testing in preparation for large-scale purchases. Major British trading firms involved in tea sales, such as Jinlong, Xiehe, and Yihang, are also taking a more active approach due to a reduction of 30,000 to 40,000 boxes in the production of Ping Shui Zhuang green tea this year, to compete for business. As a result, various types of green tea, including Zhenmei, Zhenmei, Gongxi, and Xiami, were more actively traded in the market yesterday.

Oil Market

Tung Oil Rises Slightly After Falling 258

Since the price of white tung oil soared in Hankou in July to 32 yuan per dan, foreign firms, due to the settlement of last month's futures contracts and the approaching settlement date for this month, coupled with weak spot market trading, the market was inevitably sluggish. Consequently, market prices gradually declined, eventually falling to just over 27 yuan last week. The reason for this sudden decline is that the number of futures contracts sold by various firms in August was not large, and the goods received, apart from those used to settle foreign firm contracts, still had surplus, and domestic consumption was not strong. The more it fell, the weaker it became. Recently, according to details from Hankou, foreign firms Yirui and Juxinglong purchased over 100 tons each at 26 yuan, seven jiao and five fen, with Yirui later purchasing another 100 tons at an average price of 27 yuan, according to foreign standards. From this perspective, the market has already bottomed out and is showing signs of a turnaround. Hankou firms are shipping in about 1,000 dans, priced at 21 yuan, seven jiao for customer orders, with wholesale prices at 21 yuan, five jiao. Only the lightest-colored oil is priced at 24 yuan. Currently, Hankou has over 60,000 dans in stock, most of which are intended to be sold at good prices, and are not willing to sell cheaply. Therefore, despite the large inventory, it is unlikely to affect the market. The price has already fallen to this point, and there is no risk of further decline. Local inventories in Shanghai are extremely low, and sales are good. Therefore, yesterday, various firms purchased 500 to 600 units of Zhejiang tung oil for 24 yuan, four or five jiao. It is reported that Hangzhou dealers also have little inventory, and that the producing areas along the upper reaches of the Yangtze River have sold out. The scarcity of Zhejiang tung oil in the future is foreseeable. As the heat of autumn has not yet subsided, tung oil sales are likely to continue for longer, and the market situation will remain stable. A turnaround will depend on the volume of transactions by foreign firms in Hankou.

Sugar Market

Coarse Granulated White Sugar Continues to Rise 259

Yesterday, the sugar market rose due to the exchange rate increasing to about two yuan, creating a tight situation. The association's market price for 24th-grade coarse granulated white sugar rose to two jiao and two fen after rising to 21 yuan, two jiao the day before. Yesterday, sellers suddenly demanded six jiao, while buyers offered five jiao, eventually trading at 21 yuan, five jiao and three fen. Re-export goods also rose to eight yuan, one jiao in Dutch currency (excluding taxes). 20th-grade medium granulated white sugar was priced at 21 yuan. Dutch PK brand was priced at 17 yuan, higher than the 17 yuan, one jiao offered by Gaoxiao Company. Taikoo sugar also rose by two jiao, with B grade at 21 yuan, nine jiao, CW grade at 21 yuan, seven jiao and a half, DY grade at 21 yuan, three jiao, and raw brown sugar rising to 18 yuan, one jiao. Local factory sugar rose by two jiao, Zhenji No. 1 refined sugar at 20 yuan, six jiao, Zhonghua Guohua refined sugar top grade at 20 yuan, seven jiao, No. 1 at five jiao, No. 2 at zai jiao, No. 3 at one jiao, No. 4 at 19 yuan, nine jiao, No. 1 ice sugar rose by two jiao to 24 yuan. Chaozhou merchants offered to sell several dozen packages of Qing goods for pickup at 15 yuan, nine jiao, up one jiao. In addition, there were only 20 bags of high-quality refined brown sugar available, rising by four jiao and a half to 17 yuan, eight jiao and a half. After Wufu white ice sugar rose to 18 yuan, it was reported that merchants requested a further increase of half a yuan to 18 yuan, five jiao, due to increased costs. According to general observations, the price of foreign sugar may continue to rise, perhaps because the exchange rate is expected to reach two yuan and three jiao.

Dry Goods

Golden Needles Showing Signs of Loosening 260

Recently, due to weak sales in various regions, the price of golden needles has been declining, dropping by five or six jiao. In addition, inventories are increasing, and merchant prices are becoming more flexible. Yesterday, Daxing vegetable products were sold for 16 yuan, two or three jiao, followed by prices ranging from 16 yuan to 15 yuan, four or five jiao, with the market appearing flat.

Sheet Lead Plain and Unremarkable 261

Recent sheet lead transactions have shown no progress. Tea merchants, battery factories, and others have no business, and the market relies only on small purchases from ordnance factories, publishing houses, and other entities. Prices are declining due to the unfavorable environment. Currently, No. 2 is priced at 32 yuan, No. 3 and No. 4 at 31 yuan, five jiao, No. 5 at 30 yuan, five fen, No. 6 at 29 yuan, five jiao, No. 7 and No. 8 at 29 yuan, two jiao and a half, No. 9 and No. 10 at 30 yuan. It is reported that only twenty or thirty barrels of transactions have been made in recent days.

Galvanized Iron Roofs Not Selling Much 262

Galvanized iron roofs are not selling much. The market is weak. Existing inventories are sufficient to supply the market for three months. As a result, prices are even lower than before by three or four jiao. However, the market is still slow, leaving those involved in the business feeling disappointed.

Local Factory Nails Selling Well to Merchants 263

Since the price of local factory nails returned to six yuan, nine jiao (after reaching seven yuan, four jiao), merchant business has been booming. Several thousand barrels have been shipped to Fuzhou, Xiamen, Ningbo, and various areas along the Yangtze River in recent days. However, local business has not seen large transactions. It is reported that there have been deals involving over a thousand barrels with Xuzhou, Tianjin, and other regions. The market outlook is optimistic.

Essays

"Prepared But Not Used" vs. "Used But Not Prepared" 264

— Wen Bing

In today's society, there are many things that are "prepared but not used," and there are also many things that are "used but not prepared." This extreme, left-leaning and right-leaning, deformed morbidity can be used to test the true nature of contemporary society.

Not long ago, I read in a movie magazine the wise words of movie queen XX, who said that the only way for women to maintain their beauty is not to breastfeed their children after giving birth (actually, it would be better to use more of "her friends" and completely cut off childbirth). In fact, she is very right. How many modern women are willing to give birth? How many are willing to use their own milk to feed their children? The pair of breasts naturally given to women to feed children are simply covered in powder, sprinkled with perfume, and deeply wasted. During the day, they swagger on the street to show off to the opposite sex. Human evolution has reached this point, and women's breasts have indeed become useless things that are "prepared but not used."

In fact, there are also things that are "prepared but not used" among men. For example, some wealthy gentlemen who live in the city, enjoying the grace of foreign lords, bring cars to China for their use. Their two legs are like the two breasts of modern women. Throughout the year, even for three steps, they have to use cars for transportation. The two legs that were naturally made for walking have indeed become superfluous items that are "prepared but not used."

There are many more things like this: the "flower vases" in companies and foreign firms, the mansions and villas of wealthy old men in the city during the summer (because when summer arrives, everyone goes to Mogan Mountain and other places to escape the heat, and mansions and villas are heavily locked up). Aren't these all "prepared but not used"?

Speaking of big things, it is easy to remember that at the time of the Shenyang Incident, young marshal Zhang's two hundred or so planes were also "prepared but not used." Who knew that the Japanese thought it would be a pity to abandon them, so they borrowed them all and turned them to use in the Battle of Shanghai, bombing Zhabei into its current desolate state. Capitalist countries in Europe and the United States often have valuable agricultural products such as potatoes, wheat, and soybeans sunk into the sea, simply because they are "prepared but not used." Conversely, there are just as many phenomena of "used but not prepared."

How many modern women only look up dictionaries when they need to write love letters. Most female students secretly look at books and steal from others when they are about to take exams. Some even delegate secretaries to do the work for them. This is simply the result of "used but not prepared."

What about manly men and real men? In this day and age, many people are exploited to the point of poverty and cannot even get enough to eat. However, this "used but not prepared" has a very profound and valuable meaning to study, and it is not the fault of the parties involved.

Although our country is based on agriculture, there is often a fear of "used but not prepared" when it comes to food. Last year, we suffered a vast flood that affected sixteen provinces, so of course we had to borrow from the gold yuan countries. But even in a year as bountiful as last year, food was still the top import item at customs, and we still had to use cotton and wheat loans to make up for it. Now, the Yellow River has breached its dikes again, flooding without end. I really don't know how we will survive next year. Whether it is a year of famine or a year of abundance, the agricultural country has a fear of food shortages, which is simply "used but not prepared." The specialized talents needed in general agencies and government offices, as well as the scientific talents needed in industry, commerce, and agriculture, cannot be found in the country no matter how much you search with telescopes and microscopes. The only solution is to hire foreigners to act as proxies. Isn't this also "used but not prepared"?

"Prepared but not used" and "used but not prepared" exist in so many situations in China today. What is the reason? Please forgive me, I cannot say much more.

It Was At This Time 265

— Bing

| It can also be considered one of my love stories |

It was at this time | Two years ago in early autumn, the gentle breeze was blowing, the light rain was drizzling, the weather was warm, life was warm, and I, finally, stepped from the starvation line into the circle of life.

When I moved into the small building of the X family, whom I had never met before, the reality revealed to me that it was not a human life. To put it nicely, it was like a machine to a factory owner. Because of this, I felt infinite mental distress, especially when I sat alone in the morning and evening, and especially at night, in the silent night. So I suffered from insomnia, and so I had the motivation to love.

Secondly, perhaps I was poisoned by "being full and warm makes you think of lust," and the heart when I had food to eat was different from being on the starvation line, which was undoubtedly the biggest reason for pushing the motivation.

"Wouldn't it be better if there was some spiritual comfort!"

"Wouldn't it be possible to regulate a part of life if there were a few women to associate with, without being delusional!"

I thought, I called out, and this became my self-study course during my few spare hours each day.

One day, a burst of noise suddenly came from the building across the street, interspersed with one or two familiar hometown curses. Listening carefully, I realized that they were my fellow villagers. They had probably been abroad for many years, and their accents seemed to have some northern flavor, as well as some Shanghai dialect, but after careful listening, I could determine their origin | Completely correct, they were my fellow villagers.

The second floors faced each other, and the line of sight was blocked by the two doors between them. I could only hear voices, but I couldn't see anyone. So I climbed to the third floor to get to the bottom of it, and going up another floor, I reached the sunbathing platform. At this time, looking down from a height, I could see through all the people and things there. The most eye-catching was a very delicate young lady who was rubbing her eyes.

After that, I often climbed onto the sunbathing platform, intentionally or unintentionally lingering there. She noticed this. At first, in her reported "hoping," there was a full "demonstration" of "there is a beautiful woman." I knew this was a common trick of women, and sure enough, after a long time, it was different. There were flirtatious eyes, flirtatious smiles, flirtatious greetings, and flirtatious feelings.

So I rashly wrote my first letter.

There was no response, so I sent a second and third letter······ I got a reply on the fourth letter: "I am already not a free person |" The first sentence of my reply was: "Is it true that unfree people cannot be free?" There was no reply again. I guessed that she had tacitly agreed with my words.

After that, the silent confrontation on the sunbathing platform was our way of communicating our feelings.

Not long after, she came to play at the X family, and even came up to my small building. I greeted her with great happiness and slight nervousness. She seemed a little surprised, and took a look at my simple furnishings. Then she stared at my bedding, and then was silent for a moment as if she was thinking. Suddenly she said: "Mr. X, I'm very sorry to bother you, goodbye!" This was considered her "attendance" to my boasting in the letter.

After she left, I felt infinite emptiness, infinite regret!

After that, I could only see her graceful figure from behind on the sunbathing platform.

It was at this time |

Humorous Essay

The Filthy Society of Shanghai 266

— Xu Li Qu

The Swallow's Nest

Narrow, dark, and smoky building,

A couch lies across, providing for smokers' needs.

Clearly manufacturing the land of skeletons,

But still, people linger, unwilling to turn their heads.

Prostitute

Standing against the west wind in the street,

With a powdered face, red lips, and disheveled hair.

Accustomed to welcoming and sending off strangers,

Ask her what ties her to this cage.

Small Association

Playing poker, mahjong, and douwahua,

Every gambling game appears, no gambling on credit.

How much is the salary of a pitiful month?

Do not use hard-earned money to support the family.

Loafer

Wearing a crooked hat and exposing an arm covered in tattoos,

Delivering greeting cards to make a living.

When a scam fails, they stand up,

Gathering their kind, calling out friends for a tea meeting (and reward).

"Humor" and "Archaeology" 267

— Human Nature

Literati and generals are different. "Warfare is based on deception." When generals are "locked in confrontation," they can not only use tricks like "appearing weak when strong, and causing vigilance when prepared" to win, but also "deceive with both weakness and strength." The more deceptive they are, the more honor they gain from victory. However, literati must openly discuss principles and doctrines with the public, so they must be truthful and not deceive. Deception cannot make the public truly believe. However, at certain times, not all truths can be told. Like these days, there are many truths that cannot be spoken. As the saying goes, "Disaster comes from the mouth." Now, if someone wants to honestly speak the truth arbitrarily, but they are unwilling to play deceptive tricks because they know deception does not make people truly believe, they devise a plan: to maintain the principle of not telling lies while avoiding danger. This is the origin of the current popularity of "humor" and "archaeology" in the Chinese cultural sphere.

Are there many people advocating the study of oracle bone script, Dunhuang literature, or writing "Critiques of Ancient History" and "Studies of Ancient Books"? Aren't there also many people diligently conceiving sarcastic and humorous remarks like "kick," "push," "pull," "crow," "let the women do it," etc.? This is because archaeology allows one to seriously understand historical phenomena, express some truths about events hundreds or thousands of years ago from one's own perspective without incurring unexpected danger, and also allows one to criticize Confucian corruption, Daoist elusiveness, Empress Dowager Cixi's absurdity, and Lin Qinnan's anti-meritocracy in addition to archaeology. As for telling humorous stories, although there is a component of truth and sometimes even hurts the sensibilities of great men and gentlemen, because it is close to joking and inconsequential, it won't cause any major disasters.

Naturally, in "archaeology" and "humor," literati and scholars inevitably feel lonely in the cultural world, so they take time to investigate matters of "plagiarism" and "stealing excerpts." Once they discover something, it becomes a big deal, requiring all parties to mobilize and engage in a great debate. However, generals sit aside and laugh, saying, "Literati are indeed very interesting!"

Clerk's Correspondence

A Moment of Pleasure,

Brings Eternal Calamity,

Dear Editor,

I have a question. My friend, Mr. Qiu, is just over twenty years old and works for a shipping company. Through a friend's introduction, he met a woman of twenty-nine, of average appearance. As they spent more time together, they fell in love, pledging to grow old together. Later, they frequented entertainment venues and engaged in intimate affairs. After careful investigation into her family situation, my friend discovered that she had a mother and three younger brothers to support. The family's expenses depended entirely on her, and her income mostly came from her boyfriend. Therefore, they had not formally become engaged, only exchanging a brief letter as a formality. Later, her mother became dissatisfied with my friend's small contributions, and my friend, angered, stopped seeing her. Several days later, she invited him over with a letter. My friend, suspecting nothing, went to her house. To his surprise, the family had hired thugs who tried to extort money. When they failed, they handed him over to the police. The woman accused him of rape, but the police, finding no evidence, refused to accept the case, advising them to settle it themselves. There was no further action until the other day when the woman came to propose reconciliation. My friend, fearing her malicious intentions and the potential for future trouble, ignored her. However, she constantly harasses him, and his career may be greatly affected. Feeling at a loss, he asked me to inquire of you. Considering the positions of both parties, they should bear equal guilt. But if resolved through the law, what specific liabilities would my friend face? I implore you to provide detailed guidance so that he can take appropriate action. In recent times, young people, unaware of the consequences, often pursue momentary pleasure, leading to eternal calamity. Your wise and cautionary words serve as a warning bell for society. I eagerly await your reply.

Zhu Ziming, Bell Tower

○　　　○　　　○　　　○

Editor's Note: Since your friend, Mr. Qiu, did not formally marry or become engaged to the woman, although there was an intimate affair, it can only be considered an act of fornication, without any legal relationship. Furthermore, the woman is already twenty-nine years old, exceeding the age of consent. And since it was consensual at the time, without any acts of violence or coercion, the charge of rape or attempted rape cannot be established. The only concern is whether there are seductive phrases in the so-called "brief letter." If so, your friend should bear the responsibility of seduction. If he can provide sufficient evidence to prove that it was consensual, or even that the woman initiated the seduction, then the charge of fornication cannot be established. However, if the woman is only eighteen, although she is over the age of consent, she has not reached adulthood, so in any case, your friend cannot escape the responsibility for disturbing the family. However, judging from the letter, the woman's mother seems to have the intention of profiting and indulging her daughter. It is best to collect evidence of this and preemptively file a lawsuit against them for scheming to extort money. Otherwise, he can only bear the pain and ask someone to mediate a settlement. Ignoring the matter will inevitably lead to ongoing harassment, affecting his career, and ultimately, running the risk of being convicted.

Drama

War and Peace (10) 268

— Ling He

Act One: Life and Death

Soldier Xin: Because they have money, and we don't.

Old Man: Yes, you soldiers have suffered enough, but now we are at war with foreigners, so there is no way around it. You don't know how much more we common people suffer than you do. You at least get a few steamed buns to eat every day, but we don't even have that.

Soldier Yi: Look at my leg, it's swollen like this.

Soldier Ding: Who isn't like this? Mine is even more swollen than yours. Look, there's blood coming out here.

Soldier Yi: It's infuriating. In the past, we only retreated after being defeated. But this time, fighting the foreigners is different. We only fired a few shots, didn't even make a single charge, and immediately ran. We ran so far, it's baffling.

Soldier Jia: You can't say that. Of course, we don't like fighting. It would be best if there was no such thing as war in the world. But what happened this time? We were very excited to hear that we were fighting foreigners. Everyone rushed to the front line full of murderous intent, but we hadn't even stood in the trenches for half a day before we were told to "retreat completely." If we were defeated, we didn't even see a single Japanese soldier.

Old Man: Isn't it said that the fighting at the front is fierce? Today, they brought back two truckloads of corpses and wounded soldiers from here.

Soldier Ding: Oh? I didn't know that.

Soldier Yi: So the two guys inside the temple, are they from today?

Soldier Yi: Is that so? Then I'll go ask them about the situation. (Enters the temple)

Old Man: If that's the case, if we retreat without even fighting, then what hope do we common people have? In a few days, all the soldiers at the front will have retreated, and we will become slaves of a conquered nation.

Soldier Jia: Become slaves of a conquered nation? That's too easy for you. I'm afraid you'll all become cannon fodder before long.

Old Man: That's right! If we don't want to become slaves of a conquered nation, there's only one way: to escape. But we don't have money, so we can't escape. And where would we escape to? To be honest, it's better to prepare to become slaves of a conquered nation. Otherwise, we can only wait to die.

Wounded Soldier Jia: (Comes out of the temple slowly, supported by a soldier's shoulder) I was feeling extremely sad, so I came out to talk to everyone. (Sits on the tree)

Soldier Geng: Old man, where did you get hurt?

Wounded Soldier Jia: On this side of Gubeikou, about eighty li away from Gubeikou. It makes me so angry just thinking about it. Let me tell you: the Japanese soldiers suffered a major defeat once, and we killed more than five hundred of them in one night. They didn't dare to charge anymore, just waited for reinforcements. At night, they used many flashlights, shining them like ghost fires all over the mountains. Of course, that was just a show of strength. At the same time, they used large spotlights, shining them all night until dawn. Of course, that was because they were afraid of us raiding their camp. During the day, they fired heavy artillery. This went on for almost ten days. If our officers had issued a general attack order, we could definitely have retaken Gubeikou. But we just kept defending, kept defending, until the Japanese reinforcements arrived. Tanks, airplanes, and artillery attacked us from both sides, and we couldn't hold our second line of defense. A bomb destroyed more than half of it. My leg was also blown up.

Film Special

Recent Film Industry in the Soviet Union (Part Two) 269

— Shi Chun

The Soviet Union's Foreign Affairs Commissioner, Litvinov, is a peculiar genius from Asia. The current Soviet film industry is entirely under his support. Litvinov's foreign policy includes using films to assist his diplomatic skills. The themes of Soviet films are all rich in revolutionary background, which is the minimum requirement Litvinov has for films.

In the Soviet film industry, there is a famous playwright named Chai Xi. He is the most trusted person by Litvinov. He is the master of the film industry in the Soviet Union. Most of the themes of Soviet films are adopted by him. Although he has never directed a film, all Soviet films must be carefully considered by him. Litvinov's production plans are also entirely in his hands. He is indeed the central figure in the entire Soviet film industry.

The purpose of Soviet films is not to make a profit. All of their film production is subsidized by the government. Their purpose is to promote the Soviet revolution. Therefore, once a film is completed under the leadership of the government, it will not be subject to the difficulties of film censorship in other countries. Therefore, their film production work is very systematic and bold. The ticket prices for films shown in public are extremely low. Their films are for the masses and have an educational mission.

They firmly believe that the future world war will be a conflict between labor and capital. And they say that the increase in population is a geometric progression, while the increase in resources is an arithmetic progression, so the terrifying social problems of the future are about to descend. Most of the Soviet films seize this problem as the center, telling the masses and showing them the work they are currently using to select. Although this is feared by all imperialists, in the original sense of film education, the imperialists cannot help but recognize it.

Soviet films not only openly dissect issues such as labor and capital, but also powerfully announce their revolutionary work to other countries. Recently, Chai Xi wrote several films, all of which are narratives of revolutionary work scripts. Exposing the internal work of the Soviet Union on the screen, one of the film scripts that has been written is about the revolutionary war of independence and liberation that occurred in Turkey in 1918. This film was approved by the Turkish government. Turkey's struggle against imperialism during its independence and liberation is the main historical material adopted by Chai Xi. Turkey has a trend of mutual alliance with the Soviet Union, and the revolution in Turkey is certainly tacitly approved by the Soviet Union in psychology. The expansion of Soviet films to such an extent means that their future can be self-evident. (End)

Audience Opinions

My View on "Mother and Son" 270

— Xing Zhi

After watching "Mother and Son," I feel that this film is the most failed work since domestic films changed their direction in terms of consciousness. Undoubtedly, as the giant wheel of the times moves forward continuously, there should not be this kind of film with feudal ideas.

The first thing to know is that the theme of "Mother and Son" is ill-considered. Not only is there no such coincidental fact, but the playwright's basic idea is wrong (excerpt omitted). I believe that although prison is dark, it certainly does not have the ability to change a person's face so that even old acquaintances cannot recognize them. Lin Qingyun (played by Xuan Jinglin) was sentenced to eighteen years in prison. After being released from prison, she went to her former husband He Wenchao's house to work as a servant. He Wenchao was married to her for more than three years. How could a husband and wife who have been married for more than three years not recognize each other after eighteen years of prison life? Furthermore, when Qingyun killed Long'er, the black mole on Qingyun's forehead made Long'er recognize her as his mother. Yun'er, who was lost at the age of seven, was still able to recognize his mother because of a mole, so how could He Wenchao not recognize his ex-wife? And since the black mole is on the forehead, why can Yun'er see it but He Wenchao can't see it? This kind of negligence is really absurd!

Thoughts After Watching "Mother and Son" 271

— Xian

There are several points in "Mother and Son" that are worth discussing. 1) The main switch of the lights in the Shengping Bookstore should never be easily turned off. 2) China does not yet have "female police officers," but in this film, there are several female police officers guarding the service. 3) The description says that Qingyun stole Wenchao's pistol on the night Yun remembers he订婚， disguised himself, found Gongda, and shot him, but in the picture, Qingyun went to find Gongda and shot him, which was clearly the next day in the daytime. 4) Since pistols are dangerous items, they would never be thrown casually in a drawer. In short, "Mother and Son" is not of considerable value, it is just a mediocre script.

My Review of "Mother and Son" 272

— Xiang

After watching "Mother and Son," it was undoubtedly disappointing! The plot itself is very far-fetched and there are too many coincidences, but there are also some good shots and some places that need to be discussed. Now let's talk about it briefly.

Since Qingyun and Wenchao had a good relationship, after she was hijacked, she could not just feel sorry for her beloved son and want to influence Kong Lingwu and others, so she settled down in the bandit's den. At the very least, there should have been one or two attempts to escape with her son and then been discovered and captured back before she reluctantly stayed. This would give people a deeper understanding of her personality, knowing that she was not someone who "forgot about Wenchao" and "mingled with the bandits every day."

In terms of the plot, a coerced woman is not likely to receive an eighteen-year prison sentence. The clothing and hats of prison inmates should not all use Western numerals (Roman numerals). They should be changed to Chinese numerals or a combination of Chinese and Western numerals. When a gunshot occurs in a hotel, someone should come to investigate. In reality, no one would crawl into the room to check it out after so long. In addition, the servants' bedrooms in He Wenchao's house are too elaborate! Gongda was too calm after being injured, and no blood stains were seen on his shirt. These are all illogical. (Excerpt omitted)

My Review of "Mother and Son" 273

Ding Ding

Regarding the performance in this film, I don't know how many mistakes there are. The biggest one is that Qingyun lost herself in the bandit's den because she had no choice. Afterward, she was discovered and arrested. If Qingyun could explain the reason—and of course, she could call Wenchao to testify—she would not have been sentenced to eighteen years in prison. But Qingyun didn't even think of this and obediently went to prison. I think: If Qingyun were a slightly rational woman, she would not be so stupid. Isn't this because she willingly went to prison? Of course, this plot is the most important key to the film. If Qingyun was released, the entire "Mother and Son" would completely disintegrate, so the playwright had to do this, and Qingyun was able to face trial. Therefore, the entire film "Mother and Son" was successfully completed! However, from the audience's point of view, how can this be justified?

The Trend of "Sexual Segregation" in Filmmaking 274

— Luo Fen

Since the German film "Woman" recently set a new record in the film industry, the film industries of all countries have felt the possibility of making a film with all female actors. Therefore, Hollywood is not willing to lag behind and is planning to imitate films like "Woman" with all female actors. Therefore, the so-called ideal of Sexual Segregation has now become the most fashionable problem in the film industry. Most people in Hollywood think that sexual segregation is a way to change the monotonous filmmaking method and change the taste. They all think that the filmmaking method of sexual segregation is very interesting and will at least not completely fail.

Hollywood has already started filming sexual segregation films. Paramount's new film "50 Million Women" is a film with all female actors. There are fifteen main actors in it. Sweetheart Nanette Carroll, the fleshy and attractive Carole Lombard, and Alison Skipworth are among them. At the same time, there is a film called "Gold Divers," which is a film with all male actors. It tells the story of a ship encountering danger at sea and the rescue of passengers. The Paramount authorities are still recruiting actors, and there are probably a dozen well-known male stars who will play the leading roles. There will be hundreds of men in the ensemble.

Paramount is the leader in sexual segregation. Since the filming of "50 Million Women," Hollywood has become extremely interested in the filmmaking of sexual segregation. Fox and MGM also plan to film sexual segregation films. Warner First National United Artists are also planning to take sexual segregation films. Universal is actively preparing. The films of sexual segregation suddenly became fashionable.

Soviet National Film Academy 275

— An Ding

In order to create film professionals and develop emerging film industry, the Soviet government specially founded the world's largest film art training institute——"National Film Academy." The college has a perfect equipment, a large-scale experimental photography field, factory, and a library with hundreds of thousands of books. Contributed to students experiment or reference. The entire course is divided into more than ten specialties: director, performance, photography, setting, sound, sound, chemistry, mechanics, makeup, electricity, and so on. The teachers who teach are all well-known specialists in the Soviet Union. Among the thousands of students in the whole school, there are thirty-three different nationalities, including several Orientals (Chinese, Korean) being educated.

In order to prepare for mass production (films), the Soviet Union has also opened several factories for manufacturing film, as well as sound and silent machines. I heard that the results of the products are extremely perfect, even above the products of European and American countries.

Soviet film art, like other Soviet undertakings, has made progress that is enough to amaze all mankind on earth. Looking back at my country's film industry, which is still dark and in a state of disarray (although a small part is advancing), I feel ashamed. I hope that my country's film industry can use the emerging film art of the Soviet Union as a reference, cheer up and work hard.

Joan Blondell's Advice 276

— Bing

Joan Blondell is the number one red star in Hollywood, but this time she unconsciously believes that her film screen career is not the best profession. The people of Hollywood find this very strange.

Joan Blondell recently went to Washington for sightseeing. After arriving in Washington, she visited various universities. When she was at the University of Washington, the students asked her to give a speech. She said that school is the most beautiful paradise, and I hope that you will work harder on your books. Many students now consider everything in Hollywood to be more interesting than books, but this is the worst thing. I hope you don't do this, and forget about everything in Hollywood, because entertainment is not as necessary as learning every day. As for my life in the arts, it only provides entertainment at most. If we talk about film education theory, we can only get "some benefits" during the leisure time. Joan Blondell's words are very thorough. She gave the same meaning to the students of Jefren University in Washington, so the people of Hollywood found her very strange.

Seeking 277

Mr. Tao Qixiang, No. 14, Kang Le Village, Foch Road, Shanghai, is seeking a copy of the February 6th film special of this year, and is willing to pay eight cents in postage. Damaged or late arrivals will not be accepted.

Motion Picture Novel: StranoeRhapsody Killing for Revenge, Martyrdom for Love (6) 278

— Da Ke

That evening, because of Serbia's independence, Du Sheng held a celebration at home. When the guests filled the hall, everyone felt that Du Sheng was no longer the amiable and approachable person he used to be. He was stern-faced and preoccupied. He pieced together the suspicions he had harbored during the day with all the casual signs of the past, feeling that even the slightest clues could confirm Qi Sa's crime with Ai Lina. In the middle of the banquet, the new military judge, Bang Tuo, arrived. He came to obtain an officer's signature on a search warrant to search the residences of several national enemies, and Qi Sa's name was also prominently on that list of national enemies. The guests discussed among themselves, saying that it was easy for searchers to frame someone, and that military execution was a very convenient method of disposal. Du Sheng coldly watched Ai Lina's facial expressions change from the side. He pretended to be indifferent, quietly waiting for Ai Lina to become unbearable and beg him to warn Qi Sa. He coldly waited for the facts to prove his wife's adultery, thinking that it was impossible to escape. Ai Lina was also afraid that she would be too anxious and reveal her flaws, so she also paid close attention to Du Sheng's attitude. Finally, Du Sheng ordered the carriage to be prepared, but suddenly his jealousy burned up, and he delayed going. Ai Lina was, after all, a woman, and she could no longer bear it. Suddenly, disregarding everything, she frantically begged Du Sheng to rescue Qi Sa. Du Sheng's rage immediately erupted uncontrollably, and he vowed not to care. He said that even if they were to hang Qi Sa, he would not lift a finger to save him. He also sent the carriage away.

Ai Lina said nothing, her face turned pale, she struggled free from her husband's grasp, and ran straight out. She ran across the vast fields towards Qi Sa's residence. But before Ai Lina could say a few words to Qi Sa, Du Sheng had already arrived. He cursed Qi Sa like a vicious god, saying that he was a beast in human form, a beast in clothing. He kept asking, "When did this happen? When did you get her?" Qi Sa calmly shouted, "God save me, this is completely untrue." Ai Lina also defended, "No, Du Sheng, this is not true." Du Sheng snorted and said, "No? Oh, I understand."

"It hasn't happened yet. Just kissing. Fumbling around, behind my back. Not enough yet. Still need to go further." Ai Lina suddenly shouted, "Don't say any more." Du Sheng said, "Those are all lies." Du Sheng said, "Lies? Don't you have anything going on? Haven't you even kissed? Look at me, answer me!" Ai Lina couldn't answer him. Du Sheng grabbed her and shook her, but she didn't say a word. Du Sheng lost his self-control, and the two men wrestled and fought, each using all their strength to kill the other (To be continued)

(Note: All instances of the name "Du Shu" in the above article should be corrected to "Du Sheng.")
